    83	    @Override
    84	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    85	        Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    86	        Permanent permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    87	        if (permanent == null || player == null) {
    88	            return false;
    89	        }
    90	        Card card = permanent.getMainCard();
    91	        player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
    92	        player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
    93	        return true;
    94	    }

     1	package mage.abilities.effects.common;
     2	
     3	import mage.MageObject;
     4	import mage.abilities.Ability;
     5	import mage.abilities.SpellAbility;
     6	import mage.abilities.effects.Effect;
     7	import mage.abilities.effects.OneShotEffect;
     8	import mage.abilities.keyword.EnchantAbility;
     9	import mage.constants.Duration;
    10	import mage.constants.Outcome;
    11	import mage.constants.SubType;
    12	import mage.filter.FilterPermanent;
    13	import mage.filter.StaticFilters;
    14	import mage.game.Game;
    15	import mage.game.permanent.Permanent;
    16	import mage.players.Player;
    17	import mage.target.Target;
    18	import mage.target.TargetPermanent;
    19	import mage.util.functions.CopyApplier;
    20	import mage.util.functions.EmptyCopyApplier;
    21	
    22	import java.util.UUID;
    23	
    24	/**
    25	 * @author BetaSteward_at_googlemail.com
    26	 */
    27	public class CopyPermanentEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    28	
    29	    private final FilterPermanent filter;
    30	    private final CopyApplier applier;
    31	    private final boolean useTargetOfAbility;
    32	    private Permanent bluePrintPermanent;
    33	    private Duration duration = Duration.Custom;
    34	
    35	    public CopyPermanentEffect() {
    36	        this(StaticFilters.FILTER_PERMANENT_CREATURE);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    public CopyPermanentEffect(CopyApplier applier) {
    40	        this(StaticFilters.FILTER_PERMANENT_CREATURE, applier);
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    public CopyPermanentEffect(FilterPermanent filter) {
    44	        this(filter, new EmptyCopyApplier());
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    public CopyPermanentEffect(FilterPermanent filter, CopyApplier applier) {
    48	        this(filter, applier, false);
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    public CopyPermanentEffect(FilterPermanent filter, CopyApplier applier, boolean useTarget) {
    52	        super(Outcome.Copy);
    53	        this.applier = applier;
    54	        this.filter = filter;
    55	        this.useTargetOfAbility = useTarget;
    56	
    57	        String text = "as a copy of";
    58	        if (filter.getMessage().startsWith("a ") || filter.getMessage().startsWith("an ")) {
    59	            text += " " + filter.getMessage();
    60	        } else {
    61	            text += " any " + filter.getMessage() + " on the battlefield";
    62	        }
    63	        text += applier == null ? "" : applier.getText();
    64	        this.staticText = text;
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    protected CopyPermanentEffect(final CopyPermanentEffect effect) {
    68	        super(effect);
    69	        this.filter = effect.filter.copy();
    70	        this.applier = effect.applier;
    71	        if (effect.bluePrintPermanent != null) {
    72	            this.bluePrintPermanent = effect.bluePrintPermanent.copy();
    73	        }
    74	        this.useTargetOfAbility = effect.useTargetOfAbility;
    75	        this.duration = effect.duration;
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    @Override
    79	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    80	        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    81	        MageObject sourcePermanent = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId());
    82	        if (sourcePermanent == null) {
    83	            sourcePermanent = game.getObject(source);
    84	        }
    85	        if (controller == null || sourcePermanent == null) {
    86	            return false;
    87	        }
    88	        Permanent copyFromPermanent = null;
    89	        if (useTargetOfAbility) {
    90	            copyFromPermanent = game.getPermanent(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
    91	        } else {
    92	            Target target = new TargetPermanent(filter);
    93	            target.withNotTarget(true);
    94	            if (target.canChoose(controller.getId(), source, game)) {
    95	                controller.choose(Outcome.Copy, target, source, game);
    96	                copyFromPermanent = game.getPermanent(target.getFirstTarget());
    97	            }
    98	        }
    99	        if (copyFromPermanent == null) {
   100	            return true;
   101	        }
   102	        bluePrintPermanent = game.copyPermanent(duration, copyFromPermanent, sourcePermanent.getId(), source, applier);
   103	        if (bluePrintPermanent == null) {
   104	            return false;
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        // if object is a copy of an aura, it needs to attach again for new target
   108	        if (!bluePrintPermanent.hasSubtype(SubType.AURA, game)) {
   109	            return true;
   110	        }
   111	        //copied from mage.cards.c.CopyEnchantment.java
   112	
   113	        // permanent can be attached (Estrid's Mask) or enchant (Utopia Sprawl)
   114	        // TODO: fix Animate Dead -- it's can't be copied (can't retarget)
   115	        Outcome auraOutcome = Outcome.BoostCreature;
   116	        Target auraTarget = null;
   117	
   118	        // attach - search effect in spell ability (example: cast Utopia Sprawl, cast Estrid's Invocation on it)
   119	        for (Ability ability : bluePrintPermanent.getAbilities()) {
   120	            if (!(ability instanceof SpellAbility)) {
   121	                continue;
   122	            }
   123	            auraOutcome = ability.getEffects().getOutcome(ability);
   124	            for (Effect effect : ability.getEffects()) {
   125	                if (!(effect instanceof AttachEffect)) {
   126	                    continue;
   127	                }
   128	                if (bluePrintPermanent.getSpellAbility().getTargets().size() > 0) {
   129	                    auraTarget = bluePrintPermanent.getSpellAbility().getTargets().get(0);
   130	                }
   131	            }
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        // enchant - search in all abilities (example: cast Estrid's Invocation on enchanted creature by Estrid, the Masked second ability, cast Estrid's Invocation on it)
   135	        if (auraTarget == null) {
   136	            for (Ability ability : bluePrintPermanent.getAbilities()) {
   137	                if (!(ability instanceof EnchantAbility)) {
   138	                    continue;
   139	                }
   140	                auraOutcome = ability.getEffects().getOutcome(ability);
   141	                if (ability.getTargets().size() > 0) { // Animate Dead don't have targets
   142	                    auraTarget = ability.getTargets().get(0);
   143	                }
   144	            }
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        /* if this is a copy of a copy, the copy's target has been
   148	         * copied and needs to be cleared
   149	         */
   150	        if (auraTarget == null) {
   151	            return true;
   152	        }
   153	        // clear selected target
   154	        if (auraTarget.getFirstTarget() != null) {
   155	            auraTarget.remove(auraTarget.getFirstTarget());
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        // select new target
   159	        auraTarget.withNotTarget(true);
   160	
   161	        UUID targetId = (UUID) game.getState().getValue("attachTo:" + sourcePermanent.getId());
   162	        if (targetId == null) {
   163	            if (!controller.choose(auraOutcome, auraTarget, source, game)) {
   164	                return true;
   165	            }
   166	            targetId = auraTarget.getFirstTarget();
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        Permanent targetPermanent = game.getPermanent(targetId);
   170	        Player targetPlayer = game.getPlayer(targetId);
   171	        if (targetPermanent != null) {
   172	            targetPermanent.addAttachment(sourcePermanent.getId(), source, game);
   173	        } else if (targetPlayer != null) {
   174	            targetPlayer.addAttachment(sourcePermanent.getId(), source, game);
   175	        } else {
   176	            return false;
   177	        }
   178	        return true;
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    public Permanent getBluePrintPermanent() {
   182	        return bluePrintPermanent;
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    @Override
   186	    public CopyPermanentEffect copy() {
   187	        return new CopyPermanentEffect(this);
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    public CopyPermanentEffect setDuration(Duration duration) {
   191	        this.duration = duration;
   192	        return this;
   193	    }
   194	}

  1701	    @Override
  1702	    public void playPriority(UUID activePlayerId, boolean resuming) {
  1703	        if (!this.isSimulation() && this.inCheckPlayableState()) {
  1704	            throw new IllegalStateException("Wrong code usage. Only simulation games can be in CheckPlayableState");
  1705	        }
  1706	
  1707	        int priorityErrorsCount = 0;
  1708	        infiniteLoopCounter = 0;
  1709	        int rollbackBookmarkOnPriorityStart = 0;
  1710	        clearAllBookmarks();
  1711	        try {
  1712	            applyEffects();
  1713	            while (!isPaused() && !checkIfGameIsOver() && !this.getTurn().isEndTurnRequested()) {
  1714	                if (!resuming) {
  1715	                    state.getPlayers().resetPassed();
  1716	                    state.getPlayerList().setCurrent(activePlayerId);
  1717	                } else {
  1718	                    state.getPlayerList().setCurrent(this.getPriorityPlayerId());
  1719	                }
  1720	                fireUpdatePlayersEvent();

  1728	                        state.setPriorityPlayerId(player.getId());
  1729	                        while (!player.isPassed() && player.canRespond() && !isPaused() && !checkIfGameIsOver()) {
  1730	                            if (!resuming) {
  1731	                                // 603.3. Once an ability has triggered, its controller puts it on the stack as an object that's not a card the next time a player would receive priority
  1732	                                checkStateAndTriggered();
  1733	                                applyEffects();
  1734	                                if (state.getStack().isEmpty()) {
  1735	                                    resetLKI();
  1736	                                }
  1737	                                saveState(false);
  1738	                                if (isPaused() || checkIfGameIsOver()) {
  1739	                                    return;
  1740	                                }
  1741	                                // resetPassed should be called if player performs any action
  1742	                                if (player.priority(this)) {
  1743	                                    if (executingRollback()) {
  1744	                                        return;
  1745	                                    }
  1746	                                    getState().handleSimultaneousEvent(this); // needed here to handle triggers e.g. from paying costs like sacrificing a creatures before LKIShort is cleared
  1747	                                    applyEffects();
  1748	                                }
  1749	                                if (isPaused()) {
  1750	                                    return;
  1751	                                }
  1752	                            }
  1753	                            resuming = false;
  1754	                        }
  1755	                        resetShortLivingLKI();
  1756	                        resuming = false;
  1757	                        if (isPaused() || checkIfGameIsOver()) {
  1758	                            return;
  1759	                        }
  1760	                        if (allPassed()) {
  1761	                            if (!state.getStack().isEmpty()) {
  1762	                                //20091005 - 115.4
  1763	                                resolve();
  1764	                                checkConcede();
  1765	                                applyEffects();
  1766	                                state.getPlayers().resetPassed();
  1767	                                fireUpdatePlayersEvent();

  1769	                                break;
  1770	                            } else {
  1771	                                resetLKI();
  1772	                                return;
  1773	                            }
  1774	                        }
  1775	                    } catch (Exception e) {
  1776	                        // INNER error - can continue to execute
  1777	                        this.totalErrorsCount.incrementAndGet();
  1778	                        logger.fatal("Game error: " + getId() + " - " + this, e);
  1779	                        this.fireErrorEvent("Game error occurred: ", e);
  1780	
  1781	                        // additional info
  1782	                        logger.info("---");
  1783	                        logger.info("Game state on error: " + this);
  1784	                        String info = this.getStack()

  1787	                        cat:         .collect(Collectors.joining("\n"));

  1790	
  1791	                        // too many errors - end game
  1792	                        if (priorityErrorsCount > 15) {
  1793	                            throw new MageException("Too many errors, game will be end. Last error: " + e);
  1794	                        }
  1795	
  1796	                        // rollback to prev state
  1797	                        GameState restoredState = restoreState(rollbackBookmarkOnPriorityStart, "Game error: " + e);
  1798	                        rollbackBookmarkOnPriorityStart = 0;
  1799	                        if (restoredState != null) {
  1800	                            this.informPlayers(String.format("Auto-restored to %s due game error: %s", restoredState, e));
  1801	                        } else {
  1802	                            logger.error("Can't auto-restore to prev state");
  1803	                        }
  1804	
  1805	                        // count total errors
  1806	                        Player activePlayer = this.getPlayer(getActivePlayerId());
  1807	                        if (activePlayer != null && !activePlayer.isTestMode() && !activePlayer.isFastFailInTestMode()) {
  1808	                            // real game - try to continue
  1809	                            priorityErrorsCount++;
  1810	                            continue;
  1811	                        } else {
  1812	                            // tests - try to fail fast
  1813	                            throw new MageException(UNIT_TESTS_ERROR_TEXT);
  1814	                        }
  1815	                    }
  1816	                    state.getPlayerList().getNext();
  1817	                }
  1818	            }
  1819	        } catch (Exception e) {
  1820	            // OUTER error - game must end (too many errors also come here)
  1821	            this.totalErrorsCount.incrementAndGet();
  1822	            logger.fatal("Game end on critical error: " + e, e);
  1823	            this.fireErrorEvent("Game end on critical error: " + e, e);
  1824	            this.end();
  1825	
  1826	            // re-raise error in unit tests, so framework can catch it (example: errors in AI simulations)
  1827	            if (UNIT_TESTS_ERROR_TEXT.equals(e.getMessage())) {
  1828	                throw new IllegalStateException(UNIT_TESTS_ERROR_TEXT);
  1829	            }
  1830	        } finally {
  1831	            resetLKI();
  1832	            clearAllBookmarks();
  1833	        }
  1834	    }
  1835	
  1836	    protected void resolve() {
  1837	        StackObject top = null;
  1838	        boolean wasError = false;
  1839	        try {
  1840	            top = state.getStack().peek();
  1841	            DataCollectorServices.getInstance().onTestsStackResolve(this);
  1842	            top.resolve(this);
  1843	            resetControlAfterSpellResolve(top.getId());
  1844	        } catch (Throwable e) {
  1845	            // workaround to show real error in tests instead checkInfiniteLoop
  1846	            wasError = true;
  1847	            throw e;
  1848	        } finally {
  1849	            if (top != null) {
  1850	                state.getStack().remove(top, this); // seems partly redundant because move card from stack to grave is already done and the stack removed
  1851	                if (!wasError) {
  1852	                    checkInfiniteLoop(top.getSourceId());
  1853	                }
  1854	                if (!getTurn().isEndTurnRequested()) {
  1855	                    while (state.hasSimultaneousEvents()) {
  1856	                        state.handleSimultaneousEvent(this);
  1857	                    }
  1858	                }
  1859	            }
  1860	        }
  1861	    }
  1862	
  1863	    @Override
  1864	    public void resetControlAfterSpellResolve(UUID topId) {
  1865	        // for Word of Command
  1866	        Spell spell = getSpellOrLKIStack(topId);
  1867	        if (spell != null) {
  1868	            if (spell.getCommandedByPlayerId() != null) {
  1869	                UUID commandedBy = spell.getCommandedByPlayerId();
  1870	                UUID spellControllerId;
  1871	                if (commandedBy.equals(spell.getControllerId())) {
  1872	                    spellControllerId = spell.getSpellAbility().getFirstTarget(); // i.e. resolved spell is Word of Command
  1873	                } else {
  1874	                    spellControllerId = spell.getControllerId(); // i.e. resolved spell is the target opponent's spell
  1875	                }
  1876	                if (spellControllerId != null) {
  1877	                    Player turnController = getPlayer(commandedBy);
  1878	                    if (turnController != null) {
  1879	                        Player targetPlayer = getPlayer(spellControllerId);
  1880	                        if (targetPlayer != null) {
  1881	                            targetPlayer.setGameUnderYourControl(this, true, false);
  1882	                            informPlayers(turnController.getLogName() + " lost control over " + targetPlayer.getLogName());
  1883	                            if (targetPlayer.getTurnControlledBy().equals(turnController.getId())) {
  1884	                                turnController.getPlayersUnderYourControl().remove(targetPlayer.getId());
  1885	                            }
  1886	                        }
  1887	                    }
  1888	                }
  1889	                spell.setCommandedBy(null, null);
  1890	            }
  1891	        }
  1892	    }

   236	    public boolean turnFaceUp(Ability source, Game game, UUID playerId) {
   237	        if (!this.getBasicMageObject().isPermanent()) {
   238	            // 701.34g. If a manifested permanent that's represented by an instant or sorcery card would turn face up,
   239	            //   its controller reveals it and leaves it face down. Abilities that trigger whenever a permanent
   240	            //   is turned face up won't trigger.
   241	            Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
   242	            if (player != null) {
   243	                player.revealCards(source, new CardsImpl(this), game);
   244	            }
   245	            return false;
   246	        }

   248	            // TODO: miss types, abilities, color and other things for restore?!

   253	            setDisguised(false);
   254	            setCloaked(false);
   255	            return true;
   256	        }
   257	        return false;

   269	    @Override
   270	    public int getManaValue() {
   271	        if (isTransformed()) {
   272	            // 711.4b While a double-faced permanent's back face is up, it has only the characteristics of its back face.
   273	            // However, its converted mana cost is calculated using the mana cost of its front face. This is a change from previous rules.
   274	            // If a permanent is copying the back face of a double-faced card (even if the card representing that copy
   275	            // is itself a double-faced card), the converted mana cost of that permanent is 0.
   276	            return getCard().getManaValue();
   277	        }
   278	        if (faceDown) { // game not neccessary
   279	            return getManaCost().manaValue();
   280	        }
   281	        return super.getManaValue();

   681	    private boolean checkTransformRestrictionEffects(Game game) {
   682	        for (Map.Entry<RestrictionEffect, Set<Ability>> entry : game.getContinuousEffects().getApplicableRestrictionEffects(this, game).entrySet()) {
   683	            if (!entry.getKey().canTransform(game, true)) {
   684	                return false;
   685	            }
   686	        }

   692	    }

   694	    @Override
   695	    public boolean transform(Ability source, Game game, boolean ignoreDayNight) {
   696	        if (!this.isTransformable()
   697	                || (!ignoreDayNight && this.checkDayNightBound())
   698	                || this.getOtherFace().isInstantOrSorcery()
   699	                || !this.checkTransformRestrictionEffects(game)
   700	                || (source != null && !source.checkTransformCount(this, game))) {
   701	            return false;
   702	        }
   703	        if (this.transformed) {
   704	            Card orgCard = this.getMainCard();
   705	            this.getPower().setModifiedBaseValue(orgCard.getPower().getValue());
   706	            this.getToughness().setModifiedBaseValue(orgCard.getToughness().getValue());
   707	        }
   708	        game.informPlayers(this.getLogName() + " transforms into " + this.getOtherFace().getLogName()
   709	                + CardUtil.getSourceLogName(game, source, this.getId()));

    19	public class ExileAndReturnSourceEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    20	
    21	    private final Pronoun pronoun;
    22	    private final Effect additionalEffect;
    23	    private final boolean returnUnderYourControl;
    24	    private final PutCards putCards;
    25

    28	    }

    32	    }
    33	
    34	    public ExileAndReturnSourceEffect(PutCards putCards, Pronoun pronoun, boolean returnUnderYourControl) {
    35	        this(putCards, pronoun, returnUnderYourControl, null);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    /**
    39	     * @param pronoun
    40	     * @param additionalEffect       that effect is applies as source is exiled
    41	     * @param returnUnderYourControl return under your or owner control
    42	     */
    43	    public ExileAndReturnSourceEffect(PutCards putCards, Pronoun pronoun, boolean returnUnderYourControl, Effect additionalEffect) {
    44	        super(Outcome.Benefit);
    45	        this.pronoun = pronoun;
    46	        this.putCards = putCards;
    47	        this.additionalEffect = additionalEffect;
    48	        this.returnUnderYourControl = returnUnderYourControl;
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    protected ExileAndReturnSourceEffect(final ExileAndReturnSourceEffect effect) {
    52	        super(effect);
    53	        this.putCards = effect.putCards;
    54	        this.pronoun = effect.pronoun;
    55	        this.additionalEffect = effect.additionalEffect;
    56	        this.returnUnderYourControl = effect.returnUnderYourControl;
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    @Override
    60	    public ExileAndReturnSourceEffect copy() {
    61	        return new ExileAndReturnSourceEffect(this);
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    @Override
    65	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    66	        // Creature has to be on the battlefield to get exiled and be able to return transformed
    67	        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    68	        Permanent permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    69	        if (permanent == null || controller == null) {
    70	            return true;
    71	        }
    72	        controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
    73	        putCards.moveCard(
    74	                returnUnderYourControl ? controller : game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId()),
    75	                permanent.getMainCard(), source, game, "card"
    76	        );
    77	        if (additionalEffect == null || !game.getState().getZone(permanent.getMainCard().getId()).equals(Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
    78	            return true;
    79	        }
    80	        if (additionalEffect instanceof ContinuousEffect) {
    81	            game.addEffect((ContinuousEffect) additionalEffect, source);
    82	        } else {
    83	            additionalEffect.apply(game, source);
    84	        }
    85	        return true;
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    @Override
    89	    public String getText(Mode mode) {
    90	        if (staticText != null && !staticText.isEmpty()) {
    91	            return staticText;
    92	        }
    93	        return "exile {this}, then return " + pronoun.getObjective() + ' ' +
    94	                putCards.getMessage(false, false).replace("onto", "to") + " under " +
    95	                (returnUnderYourControl ? "your" : pronoun.getPossessive() + " owner's") + " control"
    96	                + (additionalEffect == null ? "" : ". If you do, " + additionalEffect.getText(mode));
    97	    }
    98	}

     1	package mage.constants;
     2	
     3	import mage.abilities.Ability;

    10	import mage.players.Player;
    11	import mage.util.CardUtil;
    12	
    13	import java.util.Set;
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * @author awjackson
    17	 */
    18	
    19	public enum PutCards {
    20	    HAND(Outcome.DrawCard, Zone.HAND, "into your hand"),
    21	    GRAVEYARD(Outcome.Discard, Zone.GRAVEYARD, "into your graveyard"),
    22	    BATTLEFIELD(Outcome.PutCardInPlay, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, "onto the battlefield"),
    23	    BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED(Outcome.PutCardInPlay, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, "onto the battlefield tapped"),
    24	    BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED_ATTACKING(Outcome.PutCardInPlay, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, "onto the battlefield tapped and attacking"),
    25	    BATTLEFIELD_TRANSFORMED(Outcome.PutCardInPlay, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, "onto the battlefield transformed"),
    26	    EXILED(Outcome.Exile, Zone.EXILED, "into exile"), // may need special case code to generate correct text
    27	    TOP_OR_BOTTOM(Outcome.Benefit, Zone.LIBRARY, "on the top or bottom of your library"),
    28	    TOP_ANY(Outcome.Benefit, Zone.LIBRARY, "on top of your library", " in any order"),
    29	    BOTTOM_ANY(Outcome.Benefit, Zone.LIBRARY, "on the bottom of your library", " in any order"),
    30	    BOTTOM_RANDOM(Outcome.Benefit, Zone.LIBRARY, "on the bottom of your library", " in a random order"),
    31	    SHUFFLE(Outcome.Benefit, Zone.LIBRARY, "shuffled into your library"); // may need special case code to generate correct text
    32	
    33	    private final Outcome outcome;
    34	    private final Zone zone;
    35	    private final String messageYour;
    36	    private final String messageOwner;
    37	    private final String order;
    38	
    39	    PutCards(Outcome outcome, Zone zone, String message) {
    40	        this(outcome, zone, message, "");
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    PutCards(Outcome outcome, Zone zone, String message, String order) {
    44	        this.outcome = outcome;
    45	        this.zone = zone;
    46	        this.messageYour = message;
    47	        this.messageOwner = message.replace("your", "its owner's");
    48	        this.order = order;
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    public Outcome getOutcome() {
    52	        return outcome;
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    public Zone getZone() {
    56	        return zone;
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    public String getMessage(boolean owner, boolean withOrder) {
    60	        String message = owner ? messageOwner : messageYour;
    61	        return withOrder ? message + order : message;
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    public boolean moveCard(Player player, Card card, Ability source, Game game, String description) {
    65	        switch (this) {
    66	            case TOP_OR_BOTTOM:
    67	                if (player.chooseUse(Outcome.Neutral,
    68	                        "Put the " + description + " on the top or bottom of its owner's library?",
    69	                        null, "Top", "Bottom", source, game
    70	                )) {
    71	                    return player.putCardsOnTopOfLibrary(new CardsImpl(card), game, source, true);
    72	                } else {
    73	                    return player.putCardsOnBottomOfLibrary(new CardsImpl(card), game, source, true);
    74	                }
    75	            case TOP_ANY:
    76	                return player.putCardsOnTopOfLibrary(new CardsImpl(card), game, source, true);
    77	            case BOTTOM_ANY:
    78	                return player.putCardsOnBottomOfLibrary(new CardsImpl(card), game, source, true);
    79	            case BOTTOM_RANDOM:
    80	                return player.putCardsOnBottomOfLibrary(new CardsImpl(card), game, source, false);
    81	            case BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED:
    82	                return player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, true, false, false, null);
    83	            case BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED_ATTACKING:
    84	                if (player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, true, false, false, null)) {
    85	                    Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
    86	                    if (permanent != null) {
    87	                        game.getCombat().addAttackingCreature(permanent.getId(), game);
    88	                    }
    89	                    return true;
    90	                }
    91	                return false;
    92	            case SHUFFLE:
    93	                return player.shuffleCardsToLibrary(card, game, source);
    94	            case BATTLEFIELD_TRANSFORMED:
    95	                if (card instanceof TransformingDoubleFacedCard) {
    96	                    card = ((TransformingDoubleFacedCard) card).getRightHalfCard();
    97	                }
    98	                game.getState().setValue(TransformingDoubleFacedCard.VALUE_KEY_ENTER_TRANSFORMED + card.getId(), Boolean.TRUE);
    99	            case BATTLEFIELD:
   100	            case EXILED:
   101	            case HAND:
   102	            case GRAVEYARD:
   103	                return player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game);
   104	            default:
   105	                throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Missing case for " + this.name() + "in PutCards.moveCard");
   106	        }
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    public boolean moveCards(Player player, Cards cards, Ability source, Game game) {
   110	        switch (this) {
   111	            case TOP_OR_BOTTOM:
   112	                throw new UnsupportedOperationException("PutCards.TOP_OR_BOTTOM does not support moving multiple cards");
   113	            case TOP_ANY:
   114	                return player.putCardsOnTopOfLibrary(cards, game, source, true);
   115	            case BOTTOM_ANY:
   116	                return player.putCardsOnBottomOfLibrary(cards, game, source, true);
   117	            case BOTTOM_RANDOM:
   118	                return player.putCardsOnBottomOfLibrary(cards, game, source, false);
   119	            case BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED:
   120	                return player.moveCards(cards.getCards(game), Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, true, false, false, null);
   121	            case BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED_ATTACKING:
   122	                Set<Card> cardSet = cards.getCards(game);
   123	                if (player.moveCards(cardSet, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, true, false, false, null)) {
   124	                    for (Card card : cardSet) {
   125	                        Permanent permanent = CardUtil.getPermanentFromCardPutToBattlefield(card, game);
   126	                        if (permanent != null) {
   127	                            game.getCombat().addAttackingCreature(permanent.getId(), game);
   128	                        }
   129	                    }
   130	                    return true;
   131	                }
   132	                return false;
   133	            case SHUFFLE:
   134	                return player.shuffleCardsToLibrary(cards, game, source);
   135	            case BATTLEFIELD_TRANSFORMED:
   136	                cards.stream().forEach(uuid -> game.getState().setValue(TransformingDoubleFacedCard.VALUE_KEY_ENTER_TRANSFORMED + uuid, Boolean.TRUE));
   137	            case BATTLEFIELD:
   138	            case EXILED:
   139	            case HAND:
   140	            case GRAVEYARD:
   141	                return player.moveCards(cards, this.zone, source, game);
   142	            default:
   143	                throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Missing case for " + this.name() + "in PutCards.moveCards");
   144	        }
   145	    }
   146	}

     1	package mage.abilities.triggers;
     2	
     3	import mage.abilities.effects.Effect;
     4	import mage.constants.TargetController;
     5	import mage.constants.Zone;
     6	import mage.game.Game;
     7	import mage.game.events.GameEvent;
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * @author Loki
    11	 */
    12	public class BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility extends AtStepTriggeredAbility {
    13	
    14	    /**
    15	     * At the beginning of your upkeep (optional = false)
    16	     */
    17	    public BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(Effect effect) {
    18	        this(effect, false);
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    /**
    22	     * At the beginning of your upkeep
    23	     */
    24	    public BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(Effect effect, boolean optional) {
    25	        this(TargetController.YOU, effect, optional);
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    public BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(TargetController targetController, Effect effect, boolean optional) {
    29	        this(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, targetController, effect, optional);
    30	    }
    31	
    32	
    33	    public BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(Zone zone, TargetController targetController, Effect effect, boolean optional) {
    34	        super(zone, targetController, effect, optional);
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    protected BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(final BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility ability) {
    38	        super(ability);
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    @Override
    42	    public BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility copy() {
    43	        return new BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(this);
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    @Override
    47	    public boolean checkEventType(GameEvent event, Game game) {
    48	        return event.getType() == GameEvent.EventType.UPKEEP_STEP_PRE;
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    @Override
    52	    protected String generateTriggerPhrase() {
    53	        switch (targetController) {
    54	            case YOU:
    55	                return "At the beginning of your upkeep, ";
    56	            case NOT_YOU:
    57	                return "At the beginning of each other player's upkeep, ";
    58	            case OPPONENT:
    59	                return "At the beginning of each opponent's upkeep, ";
    60	            case ANY:
    61	                return "At the beginning of each upkeep, ";
    62	            case EACH_PLAYER:
    63	                return "At the beginning of each player's upkeep, ";
    64	            case CONTROLLER_ATTACHED_TO:
    65	                return "At the beginning of the upkeep of enchanted creature's controller, ";
    66	            case ENCHANTED:
    67	                return "At the beginning of enchanted player's upkeep, ";
    68	            default:
    69	                throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Unsupported TargetController in BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility: " + targetController);
    70	        }
    71	    }
    72	
    73	}

    11	public class CopyEnchantmentTest extends CardTestPlayerBase {

    13	    @Test
    14	    public void copyNonAuraEnchantment() {
    15	        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Copy Enchantment", 1);
    16	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
    17	        // Creature - Dragon   2/2
    18	        // Flying
    19	        // {R}: Furnace Whelp gets +1/+0 until end of turn.
    20	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Furnace Whelp", 3);
    21	
    22	        // Dragon creatures you control get +3/+3.
    23	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerB, "Crucible of Fire", 1);
    24	
    25	        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Copy Enchantment");
    26	        setChoice(playerA, "Crucible of Fire");
    27	
    28	        setStopAt(1, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
    29	        execute();
    30	
    31	        assertLife(playerA, 20);
    32	        assertLife(playerB, 20);
    33	        assertGraveyardCount(playerA, "Copy Enchantment", 0);
    34	        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Crucible of Fire", 1);
    35	        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Furnace Whelp", 5, 5);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    @Test
    39	    public void copyAuraEnchantment() {
    40	        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Inferno Fist", 1);
    41	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Mountain", 3);
    42	        // 3/1 Flying
    43	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Geist of the Moors", 1);
    44	
    45	        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerB, "Copy Enchantment", 1);
    46	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerB, "Island", 3);
    47	        // 2/2
    48	        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerB, "Silvercoat Lion", 3);
    49	
    50	        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Inferno Fist", "Geist of the Moors");
    51	
    52	        castSpell(2, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerB, "Copy Enchantment");
    53	        setChoice(playerB, true); // copy
    54	        setChoice(playerB, "Inferno Fist"); // copied
    55	        setChoice(playerB, "Silvercoat Lion"); // target for copy
    56	
    57	        setStrictChooseMode(true);
    58	        setStopAt(2, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
    59	        execute();
    60	
    61	        assertLife(playerA, 20);
    62	        assertLife(playerB, 20);
    63	        assertHandCount(playerA, "Inferno Fist", 0);
    64	        assertGraveyardCount(playerB, "Copy Enchantment", 0);
    65	        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Inferno Fist", 1);
    66	        assertPermanentCount(playerB, "Inferno Fist", 1);
    67	        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Geist of the Moors", 5, 1);
    68	        assertPowerToughness(playerB, "Silvercoat Lion", 4, 2);
    69	    }

The tests pass currently. But the PR description mentions a bug when using Estrid's Invocation's ability for the second time. Let me try to write a script that reproduces the issue.

First, let me understand the card better:

Estrid's Invocation:
- You may have it enter as a copy of any enchantment you control, except it gains "At the beginning of your upkeep, you may exile this enchantment. If you do, return it to the battlefield under its owner's control."

So when you use the ability the second time:
1. The permanent (which is a copy of some enchantment) is exiled
2. The card (Estrid's Invocation) is moved from exile to battlefield
3. It enters the battlefield again, triggering the ETB copy effect
4. You can copy an enchantment again

Now, the issue might be in `EstridsInvocationEffect.apply()`:

```java
Card card = permanent.getMainCard();
player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```

The problem might be that after the first exile and return, when the permanent enters as a copy again, something goes wrong. Let me look at what `permanent.getMainCard()` returns for a copied permanent.

Let me look at how the permanent is stored and whether the `card` field of `PermanentCard` changes:

   141	    protected void copyFromCard(final Card card, final Game game, boolean isReset) {
   142	        // TODO: must research - is it copy all fields or something miss
   143	        this.name = card.getName();
   144	        this.abilities.clear();
   145	        if (this.faceDown) {
   146	            for (Ability ability : card.getAbilities()) {
   147	                if (ability.getWorksFaceDown()) {
   148	                    this.abilities.add(ability.copy());
   149	                }
   150	            }
   151	        } else if (card.getId() != this.getId()) {
   152	            // if different id, abilities need to be added to game state for continuous/triggers
   153	            for (Ability ability : card.getAbilities()) {
   154	                this.addAbility(ability, card.getId(), game, true);
   155	            }
   156	        } else {
   157	            // copy only own abilities; all dynamic added abilities must be added in the parent call
   158	            this.abilities = card.getAbilities().copy();
   159	            this.spellAbility = null; // will be set on first getSpellAbility call if card has one.


    11	 * @author BetaSteward_at_googlemail.com
    12	 */
    13	public class EntersBattlefieldAbility extends StaticAbility {
    14	
    15	    protected String abilityRule;
    16	    protected boolean optional;
    17	
    18	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility(Effect effect) {
    19	        this(effect, false);
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    /**
    23	     * @param effect   effect that happens when the permanent enters the
    24	     *                 battlefield
    25	     * @param optional
    26	     */
    27	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility(Effect effect, boolean optional) {
    28	        this(effect, optional, null, null, null);
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility(Effect effect, String effectText) {
    32	        this(effect, null, null, effectText);
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility(Effect effect, Condition condition, String abilityRule, String effectText) {
    36	        this(effect, false, condition, abilityRule, effectText);
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    /**
    40	     * @param effect      effect that happens when the permanent enters the
    41	     *                    battlefield
    42	     * @param optional
    43	     * @param condition   only if this condition is true, the effect will happen
    44	     * @param abilityRule rule for this ability (no text from effects will be
    45	     *                    added)
    46	     * @param effectText  this text will be used for the EnterBattlefieldEffect
    47	     */
    48	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility(Effect effect, boolean optional, Condition condition, String abilityRule, String effectText) {
    49	        super(Zone.ALL, new EntersBattlefieldEffect(effect, condition, effectText, true, optional));
    50	        this.abilityRule = abilityRule;
    51	        this.optional = optional;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    protected EntersBattlefieldAbility(final EntersBattlefieldAbility ability) {
    55	        super(ability);
    56	        this.abilityRule = ability.abilityRule;
    57	        this.optional = ability.optional;
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    @Override
    61	    public void addEffect(Effect effect) {
    62	        if (!getEffects().isEmpty()) {
    63	            Effect entersBattlefieldEffect = this.getEffects().get(0);
    64	            if (entersBattlefieldEffect instanceof EntersBattlefieldEffect) {
    65	                ((EntersBattlefieldEffect) entersBattlefieldEffect).addEffect(effect);
    66	                return;
    67	            }
    68	        }
    69	        super.addEffect(effect);
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    @Override
    73	    public EntersBattlefieldAbility copy() {
    74	        return new EntersBattlefieldAbility(this);
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    @Override
    78	    public String getRule() {
    79	        if (abilityRule != null && !abilityRule.isEmpty()) {
    80	            return addRulePrefix(abilityRule);
    81	        }
    82	        String superRule = super.getRule();
    83	        String rule = (optional ? "you may have " : "") + "{this} enter" + (optional ? "" : "s")
    84	                + (!superRule.isEmpty() && superRule.charAt(0) == ' ' ? "" : " ") + superRule;
    85	        return addRulePrefix(rule);
    86	    }
    87	}

     2	
     3	import mage.MageObject;

     6	import mage.abilities.condition.Condition;

    17	/**
    18	 * @author BetaSteward_at_googlemail.com

    20	public class EntersBattlefieldEffect extends ReplacementEffectImpl {
    21	
    22	    private final Effects baseEffects;
    23	    private final String text;
    24	    private final Condition condition;
    25	    private final boolean optional;
    26	    private final EnterEventType enterEventType;
    27	
    28	    public static final String SOURCE_CAST_SPELL_ABILITY = "sourceCastSpellAbility";
    29	
    30	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect(Effect baseEffect) {
    31	        this(baseEffect, "");
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect(Effect baseEffect, String text) {
    35	        this(baseEffect, null, text, true, false);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect(Effect baseEffect, String text, boolean optional) {
    39	        this(baseEffect, null, text, true, optional);
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect(Effect baseEffect, Condition condition, String text, boolean selfScope, boolean optional) {
    43	        this(baseEffect, condition, text, selfScope, optional, EnterEventType.OTHER);
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect(Effect baseEffect, Condition condition, String text, boolean selfScope, boolean optional, EnterEventType enterEventType) {
    47	        super(Duration.WhileOnBattlefield, baseEffect.getOutcome(), selfScope);
    48	        this.baseEffects = new Effects();
    49	        this.baseEffects.add(baseEffect);
    50	        this.enterEventType = enterEventType;
    51	        this.text = text;
    52	        this.condition = condition;
    53	        this.optional = optional;
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    protected EntersBattlefieldEffect(final EntersBattlefieldEffect effect) {
    57	        super(effect);
    58	        this.baseEffects = effect.baseEffects.copy();
    59	        this.text = effect.text;
    60	        this.condition = effect.condition;
    61	        this.optional = effect.optional;
    62	        this.enterEventType = effect.enterEventType;
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    public void addEffect(Effect effect) {
    66	        baseEffects.add(effect);
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    @Override
    70	    public boolean checksEventType(GameEvent event, Game game) {
    71	        switch (enterEventType) {
    72	            case OTHER:
    73	                return EventType.ENTERS_THE_BATTLEFIELD == event.getType();
    74	            case SELF:
    75	                return EventType.ENTERS_THE_BATTLEFIELD_SELF == event.getType();
    76	            case CONTROL:
    77	                return EventType.ENTERS_THE_BATTLEFIELD_CONTROL == event.getType();
    78	            case COPY:
    79	                return EventType.ENTERS_THE_BATTLEFIELD_COPY == event.getType();
    80	        }
    81	        return false;
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    @Override
    85	    public boolean applies(GameEvent event, Ability source, Game game) {
    86	        return event.getTargetId().equals(source.getSourceId())
    87	                && (condition == null || condition.apply(game, source));
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    @Override
    91	    public boolean replaceEvent(GameEvent event, Ability source, Game game) {
    92	        if (optional) {
    93	            Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    94	            MageObject object = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId());
    95	            if (object == null) {
    96	                object = game.getObject(source);
    97	            }
    98	            if (controller == null || object == null) {
    99	                return false;
   100	            }
   101	            if (!controller.chooseUse(outcome, "Use effect of " + object.getLogName() + '?', source, game)) {
   102	                return false;
   103	            }
   104	        }
   105	        Spell entersBySpell = game.getStack().getSpell(event.getSourceId());
   106	        if (entersBySpell == null) {
   107	            StackObject stackObject = (StackObject) game.getLastKnownInformation(event.getSourceId(), Zone.STACK);
   108	            if (stackObject instanceof Spell) {
   109	                entersBySpell = (Spell) stackObject;
   110	            }
   111	        }
   112	        for (Effect effect : baseEffects) {
   113	            if (effect instanceof ContinuousEffect) {
   114	                game.addEffect((ContinuousEffect) effect, source);
   115	            } else {
   116	                if (entersBySpell != null) {
   117	                    effect.setValue(SOURCE_CAST_SPELL_ABILITY, entersBySpell.getSpellAbility());
   118	                }
   119	                effect.setValue("appliedEffects", event.getAppliedEffects());
   120	                effect.apply(game, source);
   121	            }
   122	        }
   123	        return false;
   124	    }
   125	
   126	    @Override
   127	    public String getText(Mode mode) {
   128	        return (text == null || text.isEmpty()) ? baseEffects.getText(mode) : text;
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    @Override
   132	    public EntersBattlefieldEffect copy() {
   133	        return new EntersBattlefieldEffect(this);
   134	    }
   135	
   136	}

2026-05-30 05:22:41,866 - INFO - swea-agent-magefree__mage-14755 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me look at the `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect` again. It uses:
```java
controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
putCards.moveCard(
    returnUnderYourControl ? controller : game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId()),
    permanent.getMainCard(), source, game, "card"
);
```

So it moves the permanent to exile, then moves the card (from `permanent.getMainCard()`) to the battlefield using `PutCards.BATTLEFIELD.moveCard()`. This is similar to what `EstridsInvocationEffect` does.

But wait, there's a subtle difference. Let me check if the issue might be that `permanent.getMainCard()` returns something different after the first exile+return. 

Let me think about this step by step:

1. Cast Estrid's Invocation. It enters the battlefield.
2. `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers. Player may copy an enchantment.
3. Player chooses to copy an enchantment. `CopyPermanentEffect.apply()` is called.
4. A `CopyEffect` is created. The permanent on the battlefield now looks like the copied enchantment but also has the "Beginning of upkeep" ability.

5. At the beginning of upkeep, the ability triggers.
6. Player chooses to use it. `EstridsInvocationEffect.apply()` is called.
7. `permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game)` - gets the permanent (the copied enchantment)
8. `card = permanent.getMainCard()` - gets the main card (should be Estrid's Invocation)
9. `player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game)` - moves the permanent to exile
10. `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null)` - moves the card to battlefield

Now after step 10, the card enters the battlefield again, creating a new permanent. The `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers again. Player may copy an enchantment again.

But wait - what happens if the card that was moved to battlefield in step 10 is not Estrid's Invocation but something else? Let me check `getMainCard()` more carefully for a copied permanent.

The permanent on the battlefield is a `PermanentCard` with:
- `card` field = the original Estrid's Invocation card
- But it has a `CopyEffect` applied, making it look like the copied enchantment

`permanent.getMainCard()` called on `PermanentCard` returns `card.getMainCard()`. And `card.getMainCard()` on a `CardImpl` returns `this`. So it should return the Estrid's Invocation card.

Hmm, but what if there's an issue with the `CopyEffect`? Let me look at `CopyEffect`:

     1	package mage.abilities.effects.common;
     2	
     3	import mage.MageObject;
     4	import mage.MageObjectReference;
     5	import mage.abilities.Abilities;
     6	import mage.abilities.Ability;
     7	import mage.abilities.effects.ContinuousEffectImpl;
     8	import mage.cards.Card;
     9	import mage.abilities.common.RoomAbility;
    10	import mage.constants.*;
    11	import mage.game.Game;
    12	import mage.game.permanent.Permanent;
    13	import mage.game.permanent.PermanentCard;
    14	import mage.game.permanent.PermanentToken;
    15	import mage.util.CardUtil;
    16	import mage.util.functions.CopyApplier;
    17	
    18	import java.util.UUID;
    19	
    20	/**
    21	 * Make battlefield's permanent as a copy of the source object
    22	 * (source can be a card or another permanent)
    23	 *
    24	 * @author BetaSteward_at_googlemail.com
    25	 */
    26	public class CopyEffect extends ContinuousEffectImpl {
    27	
    28	    protected MageObject copyFromObject;
    29	    protected UUID copyToObjectId;
    30	    protected CopyApplier applier;
    31	
    32	    public CopyEffect(MageObject copyFromObject, UUID copyToObjectId) {
    33	        this(Duration.Custom, copyFromObject, copyToObjectId);
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    public CopyEffect(Duration duration, MageObject copyFromObject, UUID copyToObjectId) {
    37	        super(duration, Layer.CopyEffects_1, SubLayer.CopyEffects_1a, Outcome.BecomeCreature);
    38	        this.copyFromObject = copyFromObject;
    39	        this.copyToObjectId = copyToObjectId;
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    protected CopyEffect(final CopyEffect effect) {
    43	        super(effect);
    44	        this.copyFromObject = effect.copyFromObject.copy();
    45	        this.copyToObjectId = effect.copyToObjectId;
    46	        this.applier = effect.applier;
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    @Override
    50	    public void init(Ability source, Game game) {
    51	        super.init(source, game);
    52	
    53	        // must copy the default side of the card (example: clone with mdf card)
    54	        if (!(copyFromObject instanceof Permanent) && (copyFromObject instanceof Card)) {
    55	            Card newBluePrint = CardUtil.getDefaultCardSideForBattlefield(game, (Card) copyFromObject);
    56	            this.copyFromObject = new PermanentCard(newBluePrint, source.getControllerId(), game);
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        Permanent permanent = game.getPermanent(copyToObjectId);
    60	        if (permanent != null) {
    61	            affectedObjectList.add(new MageObjectReference(permanent, game));
    62	        } else if (source.getAbilityType() == AbilityType.STATIC) {
    63	            // for replacement effects that let a permanent enter the battlefield as a copy of another permanent we need to apply that copy
    64	            // before the permanent is added to the battlefield
    65	            permanent = game.getPermanentEntering(copyToObjectId);
    66	            if (permanent != null) {
    67	                copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
    68	                // Apply Room characteristics since effects aren't applied to entering permanents yet
    69	                if (permanent.hasSubtype(SubType.ROOM, game)) {
    70	                    Abilities<Ability> abilities = permanent.getAbilities();
    71	                    for (Ability ability : abilities) {
    72	                        if (ability instanceof RoomAbility) {
    73	                            ((RoomAbility) ability).applyCharacteristics(game, permanent);
    74	                            break;
    75	                        }
    76	                    }
    77	                }
    78	                // set reference to the permanent later on the battlefield so we have to add already one (if no token) to the zone change counter
    79	                int ZCCDiff = 1;
    80	                if (permanent instanceof PermanentToken) {
    81	                    ZCCDiff = 0;
    82	                }
    83	                affectedObjectList.add(new MageObjectReference(permanent.getId(), game.getState().getZoneChangeCounter(copyToObjectId) + ZCCDiff, game));
    84	            }
    85	        }
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    @Override
    89	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    90	        if (affectedObjectList.isEmpty()) {
    91	            this.discard();
    92	            return false;
    93	        }
    94	        Permanent permanent = affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game);
    95	        if (permanent == null) {
    96	            if (!game.checkShortLivingLKI(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
    97	                discard();
    98	                return false;
    99	            }
   100	            // As long as the permanent is still in the short living LKI continue to copy to get triggered abilities to TriggeredAbilities for dies events.
   101	            permanent = (Permanent) game.getLastKnownInformation(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source.getStackMomentSourceZCC());
   102	            if (permanent == null) {
   103	                discard();
   104	                return false;
   105	            }
   106	        }
   107	        return copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    protected boolean copyToPermanent(Permanent permanent, Game game, Ability source) {
   111	        if (copyFromObject.getCopyFrom() != null) {
   112	            // copy from temp blueprints (they are already copies)
   113	            permanent.setCopy(true, copyFromObject.getCopyFrom());
   114	        } else {
   115	            // copy object to object
   116	            permanent.setCopy(true, copyFromObject);
   117	        }
   118	        permanent.setName(copyFromObject.getName());
   119	        permanent.getColor(game).setColor(copyFromObject.getColor(game));
   120	        permanent.getManaCost().clear();
   121	        permanent.getManaCost().add(copyFromObject.getManaCost().copy());
   122	        permanent.removeAllCardTypes(game);
   123	        for (CardType type : copyFromObject.getCardType(game)) {
   124	            permanent.addCardType(game, type);
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        permanent.removeAllSubTypes(game);
   128	        permanent.copySubTypesFrom(game, copyFromObject);
   129	
   130	        permanent.removeAllSuperTypes(game);
   131	        for (SuperType type : copyFromObject.getSuperType(game)) {
   132	            permanent.addSuperType(game, type);
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        permanent.removeAllAbilities(source.getSourceId(), game);
   136	        if (copyFromObject instanceof Permanent) {
   137	            for (Ability ability : ((Permanent) copyFromObject).getAbilities(game)) {
   138	                permanent.addAbility(ability, getSourceId(), game, true);
   139	            }
   140	        } else {
   141	            for (Ability ability : copyFromObject.getAbilities()) {
   142	                permanent.addAbility(ability, getSourceId(), game, true);
   143	            }
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        // Primal Clay example:
   147	        // If a creature that’s already on the battlefield becomes a copy of this creature, it copies the power, toughness,
   148	        // and abilities that were chosen for this creature as it entered the battlefield. (2018-03-16)
   149	        permanent.getPower().setModifiedBaseValue(copyFromObject.getPower().getModifiedBaseValue());
   150	        permanent.getToughness().setModifiedBaseValue(copyFromObject.getToughness().getModifiedBaseValue());
   151	        permanent.setStartingLoyalty(copyFromObject.getStartingLoyalty());
   152	        permanent.setStartingDefense(copyFromObject.getStartingDefense());
   153	        if (copyFromObject instanceof Permanent) {
   154	            Permanent targetPermanent = (Permanent) copyFromObject;
   155	            //707.2. When copying an object, the copy acquires the copiable values of the original object’s characteristics [..]
   156	            //110.5. A permanent's status is its physical state. There are four status categories, each of which has two possible values:
   157	            // tapped/untapped, flipped/unflipped, face up/face down, and phased in/phased out.
   158	            // Each permanent always has one of these values for each of these categories.
   159	            //110.5a Status is not a characteristic, though it may affect a permanent’s characteristics.
   160	            //Being transformed is not a copiable characteristic, nor is the back side of a DFC
   161	            //permanent.setTransformed(targetPermanent.isTransformed());
   162	            //permanent.setSecondCardFace(targetPermanent.getSecondCardFace());
   163	            permanent.setFlipCard(targetPermanent.isFlipCard());
   164	            permanent.setFlipCardName(targetPermanent.getFlipCardName());
   165	            permanent.setPrototyped(targetPermanent.isPrototyped());
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        CardUtil.copySetAndCardNumber(permanent, copyFromObject);
   169	
   170	        return true;
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    @Override
   174	    public CopyEffect copy() {
   175	        return new CopyEffect(this);
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    public MageObject getTarget() {
   179	        return copyFromObject;
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    public void setTarget(MageObject target) {
   183	        this.copyFromObject = target;
   184	    }
   185	
   186	    public UUID getSourceId() {
   187	        return copyToObjectId;
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    public CopyApplier getApplier() {
   191	        return applier;
   192	    }
   193	
   194	    public CopyEffect setApplier(CopyApplier applier) {
   195	        this.applier = applier;
   196	        return this;
   197	    }
   198	
   199	}

Let me look at the `EstridsInvocationEffect` again:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    Permanent permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    if (permanent == null || player == null) {
        return false;
    }
    Card card = permanent.getMainCard();
    player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
    player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
    return true;
}
```

The issue might be with `permanent.getMainCard()`. When the permanent is a copy (due to `CopyEffect`), `permanent.getMainCard()` calls `PermanentCard.getMainCard()` which calls `card.getMainCard()`. The `card` here is the original Estrid's Invocation card. So it returns the Estrid's Invocation.

But wait - what if there's something weird with the copy? Let me check `PermanentImpl`:

Actually, let me look at the `PermanentImpl` class hierarchy. `PermanentImpl extends CardImpl implements Permanent`. And `PermanentCard extends PermanentImpl`.

In `PermanentCard.getMainCard()`:
```java
public Card getMainCard() {
    return card.getMainCard();
}
```

The `card` field is set in the constructor. Now, what happens when a `CopyEffect` is applied? The `CopyEffect` doesn't change the `card` field - it only changes the visible characteristics.

So `permanent.getMainCard()` should always return the original Estrid's Invocation card.


The `moveCards` method for exile takes a `Permanent` object. But the `moveCards` for battlefield takes a `Card` object. The issue might be that after the permanent is exiled, the `card` variable (which is `permanent.getMainCard()`) might not be valid anymore.

Wait, let me check - `permanent` is a `PermanentCard`, and `permanent.getMainCard()` returns `card.getMainCard()` where `card` is the original Estrid's Invocation Card. The original card should still exist in the game state.

But there's another subtlety: when you call `player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game)`, it moves the permanent to exile. After this, the permanent is in exile. Then `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, ...)` tries to move the card from exile to battlefield. But `card` and `permanent` have the same ID. The card should now be in exile.

```java
public Permanent copyPermanent(Duration duration, Permanent copyFromPermanent, UUID copyToPermanentId, Ability source, CopyApplier applier) {
    Permanent newBluePrint = null;
    // handle copies of copies
    for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
        if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
            CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
            if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyFromPermanent.getId())) {
                MageObject oldBluePrint = ((CopyEffect) effect).getTarget();
                if (oldBluePrint instanceof Permanent) {
                    newBluePrint = ((Permanent) oldBluePrint).copy();
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // if it was no copy of copy take the target itself
    if (newBluePrint == null) {
        newBluePrint = copyFromPermanent.copy();
        newBluePrint.resetLockedStatus();
        newBluePrint.reset(this);
        ...
        newBluePrint.assignNewId();
        ...
    }
    if (applier != null) {
        applier.apply(this, newBluePrint, source, copyToPermanentId);
    }

    // save original copy link (handle copy of copies too)
    newBluePrint.setCopy(true, (copyFromPermanent.getCopyFrom() != null ? copyFromPermanent.getCopyFrom() : copyFromPermanent));

    CopyEffect newCopyEffect = new CopyEffect(duration, newBluePrint, copyToPermanentId);
    newCopyEffect.setApplier(applier);
    Ability newAbility = source.copy();
    newCopyEffect.init(newAbility, this);

    // If there are already copy effects with duration = Custom to the same object, remove the existing effects
    if (duration == Duration.Custom) {
        for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
            if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
                CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
                if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyToPermanentId) && copyEffect.getDuration() == Duration.Custom) {
                    copyEffect.discard();
                }
            }
        }
    }
    state.addEffect(newCopyEffect, newAbility);
    return newBluePrint;
}
```

When `newCopyEffect.init(newAbility, this)` is called, it tries to set the source of the `CopyEffect` to the `EntersBattlefieldAbility`.

```java
public boolean replaceEvent(GameEvent event, Ability source, Game game) {
    if (optional) {
        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
        MageObject object = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId());
        if (object == null) {
            object = game.getObject(source);

            return false;
        }

}
```

Maybe the issue is that after the first exile+return, the permanent's `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers again, but something goes wrong with the copy choice or the permanent entering.

Let me look at `CopyPermanentEffect.apply()` again more carefully:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {

    MageObject sourcePermanent = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId());

        sourcePermanent = game.getObject(source);
    }
    if (controller == null || sourcePermanent == null) {
        return false;
    }
    Permanent copyFromPermanent = null;
    if (useTargetOfAbility) {
        copyFromPermanent = game.getPermanent(getTargetPointer().getFirst(game, source));
    } else {
        Target target = new TargetPermanent(filter);
        target.withNotTarget(true);
        if (target.canChoose(controller.getId(), source, game)) {
            controller.choose(Outcome.Copy, target, source, game);
            copyFromPermanent = game.getPermanent(target.getFirstTarget());
        }
    }
    if (copyFromPermanent == null) {
        return true;
    }
    bluePrintPermanent = game.copyPermanent(duration, copyFromPermanent, sourcePermanent.getId(), source, applier);
    ...
```

Notice that `sourcePermanent = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId())`. The `source` is the `EntersBattlefieldAbility`. `source.getSourceId()` should be the permanent that has this ability (Estrid's Invocation).

But wait! When the card is moved from exile to battlefield via `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, ...)`, the `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers. But what is `source.getSourceId()` at that point?

The `EntersBattlefieldAbility` is part of the card's abilities. When the card enters the battlefield, a new permanent is created. The `EntersBattlefieldAbility` should have its `sourceId` set to the new permanent's ID.

But actually, there's a subtlety: when the `EstridsInvocationEffect` exiles the permanent and returns the card, the card was already on the battlefield as a copy of something else. When it's moved to exile and back, it should lose all copy effects and return as the original Estrid's Invocation card.

Now, the first time we use the ability:
1. Permanent is exiled (moved to exile zone)
2. Card (Estrid's Invocation) is moved from exile to battlefield
3. A NEW permanent is created for Estrid's Invocation
4. `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers, player may copy an enchantment
5. A new `CopyEffect` is applied

This should work fine.

The second time we use the ability (on the next turn):
1. The permanent (which is a copy of some enchantment + has the upkeep ability) is on the battlefield
2. At beginning of upkeep, the ability triggers
3. Player chooses to exile
4. `EstridsInvocationEffect.apply()` is called
5. `permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game)` - should get the permanent
6. `card = permanent.getMainCard()` - should get Estrid's Invocation card
7. `player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game)` - exiles the permanent
8. `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null)` - returns the card to battlefield

But wait! At step 6, what does `permanent.getMainCard()` return? 

The permanent is a `PermanentCard` with:
- `card` = Estrid's Invocation card (set during construction)
- But there's a `CopyEffect` applied that makes it look like the copied enchantment

`PermanentCard.getMainCard()` returns `card.getMainCard()`. `card` is the original Estrid's Invocation card. So `card.getMainCard()` returns the Estrid's Invocation card.

But what if `card` has been modified? Let me check the `PermanentCard` constructor again...

When the card enters the battlefield the first time, a `PermanentCard` is created with `card` = the Estrid's Invocation Card object. When the permanent is exiled and the card is returned, a NEW `PermanentCard` is created with the same `card` (the Estrid's Invocation Card).

Now, after the second return, another new `PermanentCard` is created. Everything should be fine.

But wait - maybe the issue is with the `CopyEffect` that's still hanging around? Let me look at `CopyPermanentEffect` line 2141-2151:

```java
// If there are already copy effects with duration = Custom to the same object, remove the existing effects
if (duration == Duration.Custom) {
    for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
        if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
            CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
            if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyToPermanentId) && copyEffect.getDuration() == Duration.Custom) {
                copyEffect.discard();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

This should discard the old `CopyEffect` when a new one is created. But `copyToPermanentId` is `sourcePermanent.getId()` - the ID of the entering permanent. Since each time the card enters the battlefield, a new permanent is created with a new ID, the old `CopyEffect` won't be discarded (because it has a different `copyToPermanentId`).

But the old `CopyEffect` should have been discarded when the permanent left the battlefield (since `affectedObjectList` would be empty or the permanent wouldn't exist). Let me check `CopyEffect.apply()`:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    if (affectedObjectList.isEmpty()) {
        this.discard();
        return false;
    }
    Permanent permanent = affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game);
    if (permanent == null) {
        if (!game.checkShortLivingLKI(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
            discard();
            return false;
        }
        ...
    }
    return copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
}
```

If the permanent is no longer on the battlefield, `affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game)` should return null, and if it's not in short LKI, the effect is discarded.

2026-05-30 05:28:57,081 - INFO - swea-agent-magefree__mage-14755 - 💭 THOUGHT
OK. Let me look at the actual `EstridsInvocationEffect` more deeply. I want to check if there's an issue with how the card is moved back to the battlefield.

Actually, wait! I just realized something important. Look at `EstridsInvocationEffect`:

```java
Card card = permanent.getMainCard();
player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```

After `player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game)` is called, the permanent is moved to exile. But note: `permanent` and `card` might be the same object! If `permanent` is a `PermanentCard`, then `permanent.getMainCard()` returns `card.getMainCard()` which is the underlying card. But the underlying card IS the same object that's being moved to exile. 

When you call `moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, ...)`, the game moves the permanent (which has the same ID as the card) to exile. Then when you call `moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, ...)`, the game moves the card from exile to battlefield. This should work.

But what if `permanent.getMainCard()` returns something different? Let me check what happens when the permanent is a copy of another enchantment.

The `CopyEffect` copies characteristics from the blueprint to the permanent. But it doesn't change the underlying `card` field. The `PermanentCard.card` field still points to the original Estrid's Invocation card.

So `permanent.getMainCard()` should always return Estrid's Invocation.

Let me try a completely different approach. Let me search for any closed issues or PRs related to this
