2026-05-30 05:29:39,617 - INFO - swea-agent-magefree__mage-14755 - 💭 THOUGHT
OK, I think the issue might be more subtle. Let me look at the `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect` vs `EstridsInvocationEffect` more carefully.

In `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect`:
```java
controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
putCards.moveCard(
    returnUnderYourControl ? controller : game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId()),
    permanent.getMainCard(), source, game, "card"
);
```

And `putCards.moveCard` for `BATTLEFIELD` does:
```java
case BATTLEFIELD:
    return player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game);
```

Which calls `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` with default parameters (tapped=false, faceDown=false, byOwner=false).

But `EstridsInvocationEffect` does:
```java
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```

With `byOwner = true`. This might cause different behavior.

But the bigger question is: what is the actual error? The PR description says the error occurs when using the ability for the second time. Let me think about what could go wrong specifically on the second use.

One possibility: After the first exile and return, the `CopyPermanentEffect` creates a new `CopyEffect`. But maybe there's a conflict with the old `CopyEffect` from the first ETB? But we saw that the old `CopyEffect` should be discarded when the permanent leaves the battlefield.

Another possibility: The issue is with the `EntersBattlefieldAbility` itself. When the card returns from exile, the `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers. But what if the ability is somehow duplicated or corrupted?

Wait, I just noticed something in `EstridsInvocationCopyApplier`:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, MageObject blueprint, Ability source, UUID copyToObjectId) {
    blueprint.getAbilities().add(new BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility(
            new EstridsInvocationEffect(), true
    ));
    return true;
}
```

This adds the ability to the **blueprint**. The blueprint is then used in `CopyEffect`. But the `CopyEffect` also stores the `applier`:

```java
newCopyEffect.setApplier(applier);
```

But the `applier` is never called again after `init()`. Let me check... Actually, wait. The `applier` is called in `GameImpl.copyPermanent()`:

```java
if (applier != null) {
    applier.apply(this, newBluePrint, source, copyToPermanentId);
}
```

And then stored in the `CopyEffect`:
```java
newCopyEffect.setApplier(applier);
```

But I don't see the `applier` being used again from the `CopyEffect`. It's just stored for later reference (maybe for copies of copies).

Now, here's the crucial part: when the permanent is already a copy (after the first ETB), and then the upkeep ability exiles and returns it, the `CopyPermanentEffect` is called again. At this point:

1. `game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId())` gets the new entering permanent
2. The player chooses an enchantment to copy
3. `game.copyPermanent(duration, copyFromPermanent, sourcePermanent.getId(), source, applier)` is called

In `game.copyPermanent()`, there's a check for copies of copies:

```java
for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
    if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
        CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
        if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyFromPermanent.getId())) {
            MageObject oldBluePrint = ((CopyEffect) effect).getTarget();
            if (oldBluePrint instanceof Permanent) {
                newBluePrint = ((Permanent) oldBluePrint).copy();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

Wait! This checks if the `copyFromPermanent` (the enchantment we're copying) is itself a copy. If we're copying an enchantment that is itself a copy (e.g., another Estrid's Invocation that copied something), then `newBluePrint` is set from the old blueprint.

But that's not the issue here. The issue is about using Estrid's Invocation's own ability for the second time.

Let me think about this differently. Maybe the issue is that when `EstridsInvocationEffect` exiles the permanent and returns the card, the `EntersBattlefieldAbility` triggers again. But the `EntersBattlefieldAbility` has `optional = true`. The player can choose NOT to copy anything. But what if they do choose to copy something? Then a new `CopyEffect` is created. But maybe there's an issue with removing the old `CopyEffect`?

Actually, let me look at this line in `CopyPermanentEffect`:

```java
// If there are already copy effects with duration = Custom to the same object, remove the existing effects
if (duration == Duration.Custom) {
    for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
        if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
            CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
            if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyToPermanentId) && copyEffect.getDuration() == Duration.Custom) {
                copyEffect.discard();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

This discards old `CopyEffect`s that target the same `copyToPermanentId`. But `copyToPermanentId` is `sourcePermanent.getId()` which is the ID of the NEW permanent entering the battlefield. The old `CopyEffect` had a different `copyToPermanentId` (the old permanent's ID). So the old `CopyEffect` is NOT discarded here.

But the old `CopyEffect` should have been discarded when the old permanent left the battlefield (via `CopyEffect.apply()`). However, what if it wasn't? What if there's a lingering `CopyEffect` that causes issues?

So `discard()` sets `discarded = true` and `used = true`. The effect should then be removed on the next check.

But the question is: is `CopyEffect.discard()` called when the permanent leaves the battlefield? Let me check `CopyEffect.apply()` again:

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    if (affectedObjectList.isEmpty()) {
        this.discard();
        return false;
    }
    Permanent permanent = affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game);
    if (permanent == null) {
        if (!game.checkShortLivingLKI(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
            discard();
            return false;
        }
        ...
    }
    return copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
}
```

If the permanent is no longer on the battlefield (it was exiled), `affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game)` returns null. Then if it's not in short LKI, `discard()` is called. So the old `CopyEffect` should be discarded.

OK. Let me now focus on a different theory. Let me look at the `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect` vs `EstridsInvocationEffect` more closely.

In `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect`:
```java
controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
putCards.moveCard(
    returnUnderYourControl ? controller : game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId()),
    permanent.getMainCard(), source, game, "card"
);
```

And `putCards.moveCard` for `BATTLEFIELD` does:
```java
case BATTLEFIELD:
    return player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game);
```

Which calls `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` with default parameters:
- `tapped = false`
- `faceDown = false`
- `byOwner = false`
- `appliedEffects = null`

But `EstridsInvocationEffect` calls:
```java
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```

With `byOwner = true`. This means the card is moved by its owner, not by the controller. But since the owner is usually the same as the controller, this might not matter.

But wait, there's another difference. Let me look at the `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect` constructor:

```java
public ExileAndReturnSourceEffect(PutCards putCards, Pronoun pronoun, boolean returnUnderYourControl, Effect additionalEffect) {
    super(Outcome.Benefit);
    ...
}
```

And it uses `putCards.moveCard(...)`. For `BATTLEFIELD`, this calls `player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game)` which is the simplest form. This eventually calls `moveCards(Set<? extends Card> cards, Zone toZone, Ability source, Game game, boolean tapped, boolean faceDown, boolean byOwner, List<UUID> appliedEffects)` with all defaults.

But `EstridsInvocationEffect` uses `byOwner = true`. Could this cause an issue?

    27	    public static boolean cast(ZoneChangeInfo info, Ability source, Game game) {
    28	        if (maybeRemoveFromSourceZone(info, game, source)) {
    29	            placeInDestinationZone(info, 0, source, game);
    30	            // create a group zone change event if a card is moved to stack for casting (it's always only one card, but some effects check for group events (one or more xxx))
    31	            Set<Card> cards = new HashSet<>();
    32	            Set<PermanentToken> tokens = new HashSet<>();
    33	            Card targetCard = getTargetCard(game, info.event.getTargetId());
    34	            if (targetCard instanceof PermanentToken) {
    35	                tokens.add((PermanentToken) targetCard);
    36	            } else {
    37	                cards.add(targetCard);
    38	            }
    39	            game.fireEvent(new ZoneChangeGroupEvent(
    40	                    cards,
    41	                    tokens,
    42	                    info.event.getSourceId(),
    43	                    info.event.getSource(),
    44	                    info.event.getPlayerId(),
    45	                    info.event.getFromZone(),
    46	                    info.event.getToZone()));
    47	            // normal movement
    48	            game.fireEvent(info.event);
    49	            return true;
    50	        }
    51	        return false;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public static boolean moveCard(ZoneChangeInfo info, Game game, Ability source) {
    55	        List<ZoneChangeInfo> list = new ArrayList<>();
    56	        list.add(info);
    57	        return !moveCards(list, source, game).isEmpty();
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    public static List<ZoneChangeInfo> moveCards(List<ZoneChangeInfo> zoneChangeInfos, Ability source, Game game) {
    61	        // handle unmelded meld cards (if something moved a melded card to non-battlefield then parts must be moved too)
    62	        for (ListIterator<ZoneChangeInfo> itr = zoneChangeInfos.listIterator(); itr.hasNext(); ) {
    63	            ZoneChangeInfo info = itr.next();
    64	            if (info.event.getToZone().equals(Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
    65	                continue;
    66	            }
    67	            MeldCard card = game.getMeldCard(info.event.getTargetId());
    68	            // Copies should be handled as normal cards.
    69	            if (card != null && !card.isMelded(game) && !card.isCopy()) {
    70	                // TODO: WTF, never worked code here. Need research possible typo: !card.isMelded(game) -> card.isMelded(game)
    71	                ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded unmelded = new ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded(info, game);
    72	                if (unmelded.additionalMoves.isEmpty()) {
    73	                    // already moved halves somehow
    74	                    itr.remove();
    75	                } else {
    76	                    itr.set(unmelded);
    77	                }
    78	            }
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        // process Modal Double Faces cards (e.g. put card from hand)
    82	        // rules:
    83	        // If an effect puts a double-faced card onto the battlefield, it enters with its front face up.
    84	        // If that front face can’t be put onto the battlefield, it doesn’t enter the battlefield.
    85	        // For example, if an effect exiles Sejiri Glacier and returns it to the battlefield,
    86	        // it remains in exile because an instant can’t be put onto the battlefield.
    87	        for (ListIterator<ZoneChangeInfo> itr = zoneChangeInfos.listIterator(); itr.hasNext(); ) {
    88	            ZoneChangeInfo info = itr.next();
    89	            if (info.event.getToZone().equals(Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
    90	                Card card = game.getCard(info.event.getTargetId());
    91	                if (card instanceof DoubleFacedCard || card instanceof DoubleFacedCardHalf) {
    92	                    boolean forceToMainSide = false;
    93	                    Boolean enterTransformed = (Boolean) game.getState().getValue(TransformingDoubleFacedCard.VALUE_KEY_ENTER_TRANSFORMED + card.getId());
    94	                    if (enterTransformed == null) {
    95	                        enterTransformed = false;
    96	                    }
    97	
    98	                    // if effect put half mdf card to battlefield then it must be the main side only (example: return targeted half card to battle)
    99	                    if (card instanceof DoubleFacedCardHalf && !source.getAbilityType().isPlayCardAbility() && !enterTransformed) {
   100	                        forceToMainSide = true;
   101	                    }
   102	
   103	                    // if effect put mdf card to battlefield then it must be main side only
   104	                    if (card instanceof DoubleFacedCard) {
   105	                        forceToMainSide = true;
   106	                    }
   107	
   108	                    if (forceToMainSide) {
   109	                        info.event.setTargetId(((DoubleFacedCard) card.getMainCard()).getLeftHalfCard().getId());
   110	                    }
   111	
   112	                    // if left half is being moved, but entering transformed, change to transformed side
   113	                    if (enterTransformed && card instanceof DoubleFacedCardHalf && !((DoubleFacedCardHalf) card).isBackSide()) {
   114	                        info.event.setTargetId(((DoubleFacedCardHalf) card).getOtherSide().getId());
   115	                    }
   116	                }
   117	            }
   118	        }
   119	
   120	        zoneChangeInfos.removeIf(zoneChangeInfo -> !maybeRemoveFromSourceZone(zoneChangeInfo, game, source));
   121	        int createOrder = 0;
   122	        for (ZoneChangeInfo zoneChangeInfo : zoneChangeInfos) {
   123	            if (createOrder == 0 && Zone.BATTLEFIELD.equals(zoneChangeInfo.event.getToZone())) {
   124	                // All permanents go to battlefield at the same time (=create order)
   125	                createOrder = game.getState().getNextPermanentOrderNumber();
   126	            }
   127	            placeInDestinationZone(zoneChangeInfo, createOrder, source, game);
   128	            if (game.getPhase() != null) { // moving cards to zones before game started does not need events
   129	                game.addSimultaneousEvent(zoneChangeInfo.event);
   130	            }
   131	        }
   132	        return zoneChangeInfos;
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    private static void placeInDestinationZone(ZoneChangeInfo info, int createOrder, Ability source, Game game) {
   136	        // Handle unmelded cards
   137	        if (info instanceof ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded) {
   138	            ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded unmelded = (ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded) info;
   139	            Zone toZone = null;
   140	            for (ZoneChangeInfo additionalMove : unmelded.additionalMoves) {
   141	                toZone = additionalMove.event.getToZone();
   142	                placeInDestinationZone(additionalMove, createOrder, source, game);
   143	            }
   144	            // We arbitrarily prefer the bottom half card. This should never be relevant.
   145	            if (toZone != null) {
   146	                game.setZone(unmelded.event.getTargetId(), toZone);
   147	            }
   148	            return;
   149	        }

   325	    public static Card getTargetCard(Game game, UUID targetId) {
   326	        Card card = game.getCard(targetId);
   327	        if (card != null) {
   328	            return card;
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        card = game.getMeldCard(targetId);
   332	        if (card != null) {
   333	            return card;
   334	        }
   335	
   336	        return game.getPermanent(targetId);
   337	    }

   339	    private static boolean maybeRemoveFromSourceZone(ZoneChangeInfo info, Game game, Ability source) {
   340	        ZoneChangeEvent event = info.event;
   341	
   342	        // Handle Unmelded Cards
   343	        if (info instanceof ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded) {
   344	            ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded unmelded = (ZoneChangeInfo.Unmelded) info;
   345	            MeldCard meld = game.getMeldCard(event.getTargetId());
   346	            for (Iterator<ZoneChangeInfo> itr = unmelded.additionalMoves.iterator(); itr.hasNext(); ) {
   347	                ZoneChangeInfo additionalMove = itr.next();
   348	                if (!maybeRemoveFromSourceZone(additionalMove, game, source)) {
   349	                    itr.remove();
   350	                } else if (Objects.equals(additionalMove.event.getTargetId(), meld.getTopHalfCard().getId())) {
   351	                    meld.setTopLastZoneChangeCounter(meld.getTopHalfCard().getZoneChangeCounter(game));
   352	                } else if (Objects.equals(additionalMove.event.getTargetId(), meld.getBottomHalfCard().getId())) {
   353	                    meld.setBottomLastZoneChangeCounter(meld.getBottomHalfCard().getZoneChangeCounter(game));
   354	                }
   355	            }
   356	            if (unmelded.additionalMoves.isEmpty()) {
   357	                return false;
   358	            }
   359	            // We arbitrarily prefer the bottom half card. This should never be relevant.
   360	            meld.updateZoneChangeCounter(game, unmelded.additionalMoves.get(unmelded.additionalMoves.size() - 1).event);
   361	            return true;
   362	        }
   363	
   364	        // Handle all normal cases
   365	        Card card = getTargetCard(game, event.getTargetId());
   366	        if (card == null) {
   367	            // if we can't find the card we can't remove it.
   368	            return false;
   369	        }
   370	
   371	        boolean isGoodToMove = false;
   372	        if (info.faceDown) {
   373	            // any card can be moved as face down (doubled faced cards also support face down)
   374	            isGoodToMove = true;
   375	        } else if (event.getToZone().equals(Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
   376	            // non-permanents can't move to battlefield
   377	            // TODO: possible bug with Nightbound, search all usage of getValue(TransformingDoubleFacedCard.VALUE_KEY_ENTER_TRANSFORMED and insert additional check Ability.checkCard
   378	            /*
   379	             * 712.14a. If a spell or ability puts a double-faced card onto the battlefield "transformed" or "converted,"
   380	             * it enters the battlefield with its back face up. If a player is instructed to put a card that isn't a double-faced card
   381	             * onto the battlefield transformed or converted, that card stays in its current zone.
   382	             */
   383	            boolean wantToTransform = Boolean.TRUE.equals(game.getState().getValue(TransformingDoubleFacedCard.VALUE_KEY_ENTER_TRANSFORMED + card.getId()));
   384	            if (wantToTransform && !(card instanceof DoubleFacedCardHalf)) {
   385	                isGoodToMove = card.isTransformable() && card.getSecondCardFace().isPermanent(game);
   386	            } else {
   387	                isGoodToMove = card.isPermanent(game);
   388	            }
   389	        } else {
   390	            // other zones allows to move
   391	            isGoodToMove = true;
   392	        }
   393	        if (!isGoodToMove) {
   394	            return false;
   395	        }
   396	
   397	        // TODO: is it buggy? Card characteristics are global - if you change face down then it will be
   398	        //  changed in original card too, not in blueprint only
   399	        card.setFaceDown(info.faceDown, game);
   400

2026-05-30 05:30:51,886 - INFO - swea-agent-magefree__mage-14755 - 💭 THOUGHT
This is very long. Let me focus on the issue at hand.

I've been going through a lot of code. Let me step back and think about what the actual bug might be.

The PR description says:
- "xmage - game error with Estrid's Invocation's ability using for the second time"
- "Estrid's Invocation causes a fatal error when using its ability in the second turn its on the battlefield"

So the error happens when the ability is used the second time. The first time works fine.

Let me think about what's different between the first and second use:

First use:
1. Estrid's Invocation was cast and entered the battlefield as a copy of some enchantment
2. At the beginning of upkeep, the ability triggers
3. The permanent is exiled and returned
4. It enters as a new copy (player may choose a new enchantment to copy)

Second use:
1. Estrid's Invocation is on the battlefield as a copy (from the first use's return)
2. At the beginning of upkeep, the ability triggers
3. The permanent is exiled and returned
4. It should enter as a new copy again

What could be different? Let me look at the `CopyPermanentEffect` handling of copies of copies.

In `GameImpl.copyPermanent()`:
```java
for (Effect effect : getState().getContinuousEffects().getLayeredEffects(this)) {
    if (effect instanceof CopyEffect) {
        CopyEffect copyEffect = (CopyEffect) effect;
        if (copyEffect.getSourceId().equals(copyFromPermanent.getId())) {
            MageObject oldBluePrint = ((CopyEffect) effect).getTarget();
            if (oldBluePrint instanceof Permanent) {
                newBluePrint = ((Permanent) oldBluePrint).copy();
            }
        }
    }
}
```

This checks if the enchantment we're copying (`copyFromPermanent`) is itself a copy. If the player chooses to copy the same enchantment again, and that enchantment is not a copy, this won't trigger.

But what if the player copies a different enchantment? Or what if the original enchantment they copied was removed?

Actually, wait. What if the issue is simpler? Let me look at `EstridsInvocationEffect`:

```java
Card card = permanent.getMainCard();
player.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```

After `moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, ...)`, the permanent is in exile. Then `moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, ...)` moves the card from exile to battlefield. But `card` is `permanent.getMainCard()`. If the permanent was a `PermanentCard`, then `permanent.getMainCard()` returns the underlying card. But if for some reason the permanent was something else (like a copy of a copy), maybe `getMainCard()` returns something unexpected?

Wait, I just thought of something. What if the issue is that `permanent.getMainCard()` returns the card, but the card and the permanent have the SAME ID? When you exile the permanent, both the permanent and the card are in exile (they're the same object). Then when you move the card to the battlefield, it works.

But what if the permanent is a token? No, Estrid's Invocation is not a token.

Let me look at another card that has similar functionality - `Frenetic Sliver`:

    16	public class ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect extends OneShotEffect {
    17	
    18	    private final boolean returnTapped;
    19	
    20	    public ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect() {
    21	        this(false);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    /**
    25	     * @param returnTapped Does the source return tapped to the battlefield
    26	     */
    27	    public ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect(boolean returnTapped) {
    28	        super(Outcome.Benefit);
    29	        this.returnTapped = returnTapped;
    30	        staticText = "exile {this}. Return it to the battlefield " + (returnTapped ? "tapped " : "") +
    31	                "under its owner's control at the beginning of the next end step";
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    public ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect(ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect effect) {
    35	        super(effect);
    36	        this.returnTapped = effect.returnTapped;
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    @Override
    40	    public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    41	        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    42	        if (controller == null) {
    43	            return false;
    44	        }
    45	        Permanent permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    46	        if (permanent == null) {
    47	            return true;
    48	        }
    49	        controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);
    50	        //create delayed triggered ability and return it from every public zone it was next moved to
    51	        game.addDelayedTriggeredAbility(new AtTheBeginOfNextEndStepDelayedTriggeredAbility(
    52	                new ReturnToBattlefieldUnderOwnerControlTargetEffect(returnTapped, false)
    53	                        .setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(permanent.getId(), game))
    54	        ), source);
    55	        return true;
    56	    }

```java
case EXILED:
    // old logic that directly adds a card to exile zone
    for (Card card : cards) {
        fromZone = game.getState().getZone(card.getId());
        ZoneChangeEvent event = new ZoneChangeEvent(card.getId(), source,
                byOwner ? card.getOwnerId() : getId(), fromZone, Zone.EXILED, appliedEffects);
        ZoneChangeInfo.Exile info = new ZoneChangeInfo.Exile(event);
        if (ZonesHandler.moveCard(info, game, source)) {
            successfulMovedCards.add(card);
        }
    }
    game.applyEffects(); // without LKI reset
    break;
```

And in `ZonesHandler.moveCard`:
```java
public static boolean moveCard(ZoneChangeInfo info, Game game, Ability source) {
    List<ZoneChangeInfo> list = new ArrayList<>();
    list.add(info);
    return !moveCards(list, source, game).isEmpty();
}
```

And `ZonesHandler.moveCards` calls `maybeRemoveFromSourceZone` and then `placeInDestinationZone`.

package org.mage.test.cards.copy;

import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
import mage.constants.Zone;
import org.junit.Test;
import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;

/**
 * @author test
 */
public class EstridTest extends CardTestPlayerBase {

    @Test
    public void testEstridsInvocationSecondUse() {
        // Estrid's Invocation {2}{U}
        // You may have Estrid's Invocation enter the battlefield as a copy of any enchantment you control,
        // except it gains "At the beginning of your upkeep, you may exile this enchantment.
        // If you do, return it to the battlefield under its owner's control."
        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
        // Enchantment - Aura
        // Enchant creature
        // Enchanted creature gets +1/+1 and has flying.
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Angelic Gift", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 1);

        // Cast Estrid's Invocation, choose to copy Angelic Gift
        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        // Turn 2 upkeep - use the ability to exile and return
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        // Turn 4 upkeep - use the ability again (second time)
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
        setStrictChooseMode(true);
        execute();

        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 2 + 2, 2 + 2); // +2/+2 from two Angelic Gifts
    }
}
EOF

But Angelic Gift is already attached to something (probably Grizzly Bears). When Estrid's Invocation enters as a copy, it should attach to a new target.

But the log says Angelic Gift was put into graveyard. That's the ORIGINAL Angelic Gift, not the copy. This might be a bug in my test setup - maybe the copy effect somehow caused the original to be sacrificed because an Aura can't be attached to two things?

Actually, I think the issue might be that Angelic Gift is an Aura that enchants a creature. When Estrid's Invocation copies it, it becomes an Aura too and needs to attach to something. But there's only one Grizzly Bears. If the copy also tries to attach to Grizzly Bears, the original Angelic Gift might fall off?

No, that shouldn't happen. Multiple Auras can be attached to the same creature.

Let me simplify the test. Instead of using an Aura, let me use a non-Aura enchantment:







🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/EstridTest2.java << 'EOF'
package org.mage.test.cards.copy;

import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
import mage.constants.Zone;
import org.junit.Test;
import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;

public class EstridTest2 extends CardTestPlayerBase {

    @Test
    public void testEstridsInvocationSecondUse() {
        // Estrid's Invocation
        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
        // Crusade - Enchantment: White creatures get +1/+1.
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Crusade", 1);

        // Cast Estrid's Invocation, copying Crusade
        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Crusade"); // Copy Crusade

        // Turn 3 upkeep (PlayerA's next turn) - use the ability
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
        // After return, choose to copy Crusade again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Crusade"); // Copy Crusade

        // Turn 5 upkeep (PlayerA's turn after that) - use the ability again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
        // After return, choose to copy Crusade again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Crusade"); // Copy Crusade

        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
        setStrictChooseMode(true);
        execute();

        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
    }
}
EOF

```java
public boolean replaceEvent(GameEvent event, Ability source, Game game) {
    if (optional) {
        Player controller = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
        MageObject object = game.getPermanentEntering(source.getSourceId());
        if (object == null) {
            object = game.getObject(source);

        if (stackObject instanceof Spell) {
            entersBySpell = (Spell) stackObject;

    for (Effect effect : baseEffects) {
        if (effect instanceof ContinuousEffect) {
            game.addEffect((ContinuousEffect) effect, source);
        } else {
            if (entersBySpell != null) {
                effect.setValue(SOURCE_CAST_SPELL_ABILITY, entersBySpell.getSpellAbility());
            }
            effect.setValue("appliedEffects", event.getAppliedEffects());
            effect.apply(game, source);
        }
    }
    return false;
}
```

     1	package mage.abilities.triggers;
     2	
     3	import mage.abilities.TriggeredAbilityImpl;
     4	import mage.abilities.effects.Effect;
     5	import mage.constants.TargetController;
     6	import mage.constants.Zone;
     7	import mage.game.Game;
     8	import mage.game.events.GameEvent;
     9	import mage.game.permanent.Permanent;
    10	import mage.players.Player;
    11	import mage.target.targetpointer.FixedTarget;
    12	
    13	import java.util.UUID;
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * @author xenohedron
    17	 */
    18	public abstract class AtStepTriggeredAbility extends TriggeredAbilityImpl {
    19	
    20	    protected final TargetController targetController;
    21	    private Boolean setTargetPointer; // null for default behavior (set target pointer if no targets)
    22	
    23	    protected AtStepTriggeredAbility(Zone zone, TargetController targetController, Effect effect, boolean optional) {
    24	        super(zone, effect, optional);
    25	        this.targetController = targetController;
    26	        setTriggerPhrase(generateTriggerPhrase());
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    protected AtStepTriggeredAbility(final AtStepTriggeredAbility ability) {
    30	        super(ability);
    31	        this.targetController = ability.targetController;
    32	        this.setTargetPointer = ability.setTargetPointer;
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    @Override
    36	    public boolean checkTrigger(GameEvent event, Game game) {
    37	        if (checkTargetController(event, game)) {
    38	            setTargetPointerIfNeeded(event.getPlayerId());
    39	            return true;
    40	        }
    41	        return false;
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    private boolean checkTargetController(GameEvent event, Game game) {
    45	        switch (targetController) {
    46	            case YOU:
    47	                return isControlledBy(event.getPlayerId());
    48	            case NOT_YOU:
    49	                return !isControlledBy(event.getPlayerId());
    50	            case ANY:
    51	            case NEXT:
    52	            case EACH_PLAYER:
    53	                return true;
    54	            case OPPONENT:
    55	                Player player = game.getPlayer(getControllerId());
    56	                return player != null && player.hasOpponent(event.getPlayerId(), game);
    57	            case ENCHANTED:
    58	                Permanent permanent = getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    59	                return permanent != null && game.isActivePlayer(permanent.getAttachedTo());
    60	            case CONTROLLER_ATTACHED_TO:
    61	                Permanent attachment = getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);
    62	                if (attachment == null) {
    63	                    return false;
    64	                }
    65	                Permanent attachedTo = game.getPermanent(attachment.getAttachedTo());
    66	                return attachedTo != null && game.isActivePlayer(attachedTo.getControllerId());
    67	            case MONARCH:
    68	                return event.getPlayerId().equals(game.getMonarchId());
    69	            default:
    70	                throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Unsupported TargetController in AtStepTriggeredAbility: " + targetController);
    71	        }
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    /**
    75	     * In rare cases, if the default behavior (of setting the target pointer to the active player id
    76	     * if and only if there are no targets) is not adequate, manually specify whether target pointer should be set
    77	     */
    78	    public AtStepTriggeredAbility withTargetPointerSet(boolean setTargetPointer) {
    79	        this.setTargetPointer = setTargetPointer;
    80	        return this;
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    private void setTargetPointerIfNeeded(UUID playerId) {
    84	        if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(setTargetPointer) || (setTargetPointer == null && getTargets().isEmpty())) {
    85	            this.getEffects().setTargetPointer(new FixedTarget(playerId));
    86	        }
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    protected abstract String generateTriggerPhrase();
    90	
    91	}

   440	    public Ability addAbility(Ability ability, UUID sourceId, Game game) {
   441	        return addAbility(ability, sourceId, game, false);
   442	    }
   443	
   444	    /**
   445	     * @param ability            The ability to be added
   446	     * @param sourceId           id of the source doing the added (for the effect created to add it)
   447	     * @param game
   448	     * @param fromExistingObject if copying abilities from an existing source then must ignore sub-abilities because they're already on the source object
   449	     *                           Otherwise sub-abilities will be added twice to the resulting object
   450	     * @return The newly added ability copy
   451	     */
   452	    @Override
   453	    public Ability addAbility(Ability ability, UUID sourceId, Game game, boolean fromExistingObject) {
   454	        // singleton abilities -- only one instance
   455	        // other abilities -- any amount of instances
   456	        if (!abilities.containsKey(ability.getId())) {
   457	            Ability copyAbility = ability.copy();
   458	            copyAbility.newId(); // needed so that source can get an ability multiple times (e.g. Raging Ravine)
   459	            copyAbility.setControllerId(controllerId);
   460	            copyAbility.setSourceId(objectId);
   461	            // triggered abilities must be added to the state().triggers
   462	            // still as long as the prev. permanent is known to the LKI (e.g. Showstopper) so gained dies triggered ability will trigger
   463	            if (game != null) {
   464	                // game is null in cards viewer window (MageBook)
   465	                game.getState().addAbility(copyAbility, sourceId, this);
   466	            }
   467	            abilities.add(copyAbility);
   468	            if (!fromExistingObject) {
   469	                abilities.addAll(copyAbility.getSubAbilities());
   470	            }
   471	            return copyAbility;
   472	        }
   473	        return null;
   474	    }


Notice that `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect` uses `putCards.moveCard()` which internally calls `player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game)` with default parameters. But `EstridsInvocationEffect` uses `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null)` with `byOwner = true`.

What if the issue is that `byOwner = true` causes problems when the card is moved from exile? Let me check if there's a difference in behavior...

Actually, let me look at `PutCards.BATTLEFIELD.moveCard`:
```java
case BATTLEFIELD:
    return player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game);
```

This calls `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game)` which has defaults: `tapped=false, faceDown=false, byOwner=false, appliedEffects=null`.

The difference is `byOwner`. Let me check what `byOwner` does in `moveCards`. Looking at line 4981-4982:
```java
ZoneChangeEvent event = new ZoneChangeEvent(card.getId(), source,
    byOwner ? card.getOwnerId() : getId(), fromZone, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, appliedEffects);
```

So `byOwner` affects the player ID in the zone change event. If `byOwner = true`, the event says the owner moved the card. If `byOwner = false`, the event says the controller (the player calling `moveCards`) moved it.

```java
// if object is a copy of an aura, it needs to attach again for new target
if (!bluePrintPermanent.hasSubtype(SubType.AURA, game)) {
    return true;
}
// permanent can be attached (Estrid's Mask) or enchant (Utopia Sprawl)
// TODO: fix Animate Dead -- it's can't be copied (can't retarget)
Outcome auraOutcome = Outcome.BoostCreature;
Target auraTarget = null;

// attach - search effect in spell ability
for (Ability ability : bluePrintPermanent.getAbilities()) {
    if (!(ability instanceof SpellAbility)) {
        continue;
    }
    auraOutcome = ability.getEffects().getOutcome(ability);
    for (Effect effect : ability.getEffects()) {
        if (!(effect instanceof AttachEffect)) {
            continue;
        }
        if (bluePrintPermanent.getSpellAbility().getTargets().size() > 0) {
            auraTarget = bluePrintPermanent.getSpellAbility().getTargets().get(0);
        }
    }
}

// enchant - search in all abilities
if (auraTarget == null) {
    for (Ability ability : bluePrintPermanent.getAbilities()) {
        if (!(ability instanceof EnchantAbility)) {
            continue;
        }
        auraOutcome = ability.getEffects().getOutcome(ability);
        if (ability.getTargets().size() > 0) {
            auraTarget = ability.getTargets().get(0);
        }
    }
}

if (auraTarget == null) {
    return true;
}
// clear selected target
if (auraTarget.getFirstTarget() != null) {
    auraTarget.remove(auraTarget.getFirstTarget());
}

// select new target
auraTarget.withNotTarget(true);

UUID targetId = (UUID) game.getState().getValue("attachTo:" + sourcePermanent.getId());
if (targetId == null) {
    if (!controller.choose(auraOutcome, auraTarget, source, game)) {
        return true;
    }
    targetId = auraTarget.getFirstTarget();
}

Permanent targetPermanent = game.getPermanent(targetId);
Player targetPlayer = game.getPlayer(targetId);
if (targetPermanent != null) {
    targetPermanent.addAttachment(sourcePermanent.getId(), source, game);
} else if (targetPlayer != null) {
    targetPlayer.addAttachment(sourcePermanent.getId(), source, game);
} else {
    return false;
}
```

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    if (affectedObjectList.isEmpty()) {
        this.discard();
        return false;
    }
    Permanent permanent = affectedObjectList.get(0).getPermanent(game);
    if (permanent == null) {
        if (!game.checkShortLivingLKI(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD)) {
            discard();
            return false;
        }
        permanent = (Permanent) game.getLastKnownInformation(getSourceId(), Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source.getStackMomentSourceZCC());
        if (permanent == null) {
            discard();
            return false;
        }
    }
    return copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
}
```

```java
    affectedObjectList.add(new MageObjectReference(permanent, game));
} else if (source.getAbilityType() == AbilityType.STATIC) {
    permanent = game.getPermanentEntering(copyToObjectId);
    if (permanent != null) {
        copyToPermanent(permanent, game, source);
        ...
        affectedObjectList.add(new MageObjectReference(permanent.getId(), game.getState().getZoneChangeCounter(copyToObjectId) + ZCCDiff, game));
    }
}
```

For a static ability (like `EntersBattlefieldAbility`), if `game.getPermanent(copyToObjectId)` returns null (because the permanent hasn't entered yet), it uses `game.getPermanentEntering(copyToObjectId)` and creates a `MageObjectReference` with the permanent's ID and zone change counter.

The `MageObjectReference.getPermanent(game)` method should return null when the permanent is no longer on the battlefield.

OK, I'm going to take a completely different approach. Let me look at what changes might have been made to fix this issue in the real XMage project. Since this is a PR, the fix should be somewhere.

Let me examine the `EstridsInvocationEffect` more carefully. I notice that it uses `player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null)` with `byOwner = true`. But the card text says "return it to the battlefield under its owner's control." So `byOwner = true` makes sense.

But wait, let me look at the `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect`:
```java
putCards.moveCard(
    returnUnderYourControl ? controller : game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId()),
    permanent.getMainCard(), source, game, "card"
);
```

When `returnUnderYourControl` is false (default), it uses `game.getPlayer(permanent.getOwnerId())` to move the card. So it's the owner who moves it. This is similar to `byOwner = true`.

But `putCards.moveCard` for `BATTLEFIELD` calls `player.moveCards(card, this.zone, source, game)` with default `byOwner = false`. So even though the owner player is calling `moveCards`, `byOwner` is false!

This means in `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect`, `byOwner` is false even though the owner is moving the card. But in `EstridsInvocationEffect`, `byOwner` is true.

Is this a bug? Let me check what `byOwner` affects...

In `PlayerImpl.moveCards()`:
```java
ZoneChangeEvent event = new ZoneChangeEvent(card.getId(), source,
    byOwner ? card.getOwnerId() : getId(), fromZone, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, appliedEffects);
```

`byOwner` changes the player ID in the event. If `byOwner = true`, the event says the owner moved the card. If `byOwner = false`, the event says the current player (who called moveCards) moved the card.

In `EstridsInvocationEffect`, the card is moved by the controller (who is usually also the owner). But with `byOwner = true`, the event says the owner moved it. In `ExileAndReturnSourceEffect`, the card is moved by the owner player object, but `byOwner = false`, so the event says the owner player moved it.

Both should result in the same event (owner moves it). So this shouldn't cause a crash.

Actually, wait. In `EstridsInvocationEffect`:
```java
player.moveCards(card, Zone.BATTLEFIELD, source, game, false, false, true, null);
```
`player` is `game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId())` - the controller. But with `byOwner = true`, the event uses `card.getOwnerId()`. This should be fine.

Hmm, let me look at this from yet another angle. Maybe the issue is that when the `EstridsInvocationEffect` is called the second time, the `source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game)` returns something unexpected.

The `source` here is the `BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility`. This ability was added to the permanent by the `CopyEffect`. The ability's `sourceId` should be the permanent's ID.

But wait! The `BeginningOfUpkeepTriggeredAbility` was added to the **blueprint**, which was then used to create the `CopyEffect`. In `CopyEffect.copyToPermanent()`:

```java
permanent.removeAllAbilities(source.getSourceId(), game);
if (copyFromObject instanceof Permanent) {
    for (Ability ability : ((Permanent) copyFromObject).getAbilities(game)) {
        permanent.addAbility(ability, getSourceId(), game, true);
    }
}
```

The abilities are copied from the blueprint (which is a `Permanent`). `permanent.addAbility(ability, getSourceId(), game, true)` is called. In `addAbility`:

```java
Ability copyAbility = ability.copy();
copyAbility.newId();
copyAbility.setControllerId(controllerId);
copyAbility.setSourceId(objectId);
```

So the new ability gets a new ID, the controller is set to the permanent's controller, and the source ID is set to the permanent's ID. This is correct.

Now, when this ability triggers, `source.getSourceId()` returns `objectId` which is the permanent's ID. `source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game)` should return the permanent.

I'm stuck. Let me try to find the actual fix by looking at what similar cards do differently.

```java
public boolean apply(Game game, Ability source) {
    Player player = game.getPlayer(source.getControllerId());
    Permanent perm = game.getPermanent(source.getSourceId());
    if (player == null || perm == null) {
        return false;
    }
    if (player.flipCoin(source, game, true)) {
        return new ExileReturnBattlefieldOwnerNextEndStepSourceEffect().apply(game, source);
    } else {
        return perm.sacrifice(source, game);
    }
}
```

It uses `game.getPermanent(source.getSourceId())` instead of `source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game)`.

```java
Permanent permanent = source.getSourcePermanentIfItStillExists(game);

    return true;

controller.moveCards(permanent, Zone.EXILED, source, game);

), source);
```

package org.mage.test.cards.copy;

import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
import mage.constants.Zone;
import org.junit.Test;
import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;

public class EstridTest3 extends CardTestPlayerBase {

    @Test
    public void testEstridsInvocationMultipleUses() {
        // Estrid's Invocation
        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
        // Glorious Anthem - Enchantment: Creatures you control get +1/+1.
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Glorious Anthem", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 1);

        // Turn 1: Cast Estrid's Invocation, copy Glorious Anthem
        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this

        // Turn 3 upkeep (PlayerA's next turn): Use ability
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this

        // Turn 5 upkeep: Use ability again (second time)
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this

        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
        setStrictChooseMode(true);
        execute();

        // Should have 2 Glorious Anthems (the original + Estrid's Invocation as a copy)
        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Glorious Anthem", 2);
        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 4, 4); // 2 base + 2 from two Anthems
    }
}

package org.mage.test.cards.copy;

import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
import mage.constants.Zone;
import org.junit.Test;
import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;

public class EstridTest4 extends CardTestPlayerBase {

    @Test
    public void testEstridsInvocationWithAuraMultipleUses() {
        // Estrid's Invocation
        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
        // Rancor - Enchantment - Aura: Enchant creature, Enchanted creature gets +2/+0 and has trample.
        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Rancor", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Forest", 1);
        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 1);

        // Turn 1: Cast Rancor on Grizzly Bears
        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Rancor", "Grizzly Bears");
        
        // Turn 1: Cast Estrid's Invocation, copy Rancor
        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Rancor"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        // Turn 3 upkeep: Use ability
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Rancor"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        // Turn 5 upkeep: Use ability again (second time)
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
        
        // After return, choose to copy again
        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
        setChoice(playerA, "Rancor"); // Copy this
        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears

        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
        setStrictChooseMode(true);
        execute();

        // Should have 2 Rancors (the original + Estrid's Invocation as a copy)
        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Rancor", 2);
        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 2 + 4, 2); // 2 base + 4 from two Rancors
    }
}

+package org.mage.test.cards.copy;
+
+import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
+import mage.constants.Zone;
+import org.junit.Test;
+import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;
+
+/**
+ * @author test
+ */
+public class EstridTest extends CardTestPlayerBase {
+
+    @Test
+    public void testEstridsInvocationSecondUse() {
+        // Estrid's Invocation {2}{U}
+        // You may have Estrid's Invocation enter the battlefield as a copy of any enchantment you control,
+        // except it gains "At the beginning of your upkeep, you may exile this enchantment.
+        // If you do, return it to the battlefield under its owner's control."
+        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
+        // Enchantment - Aura
+        // Enchant creature
+        // Enchanted creature gets +1/+1 and has flying.
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Angelic Gift", 1);
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 1);
+
+        // Cast Estrid's Invocation, choose to copy Angelic Gift
+        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
+        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears
+
+        // Turn 2 upkeep - use the ability to exile and return
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
+        
+        // After return, choose to copy again
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
+        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears
+
+        // Turn 4 upkeep - use the ability again (second time)
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the upkeep ability
+        
+        // After return, choose to copy again
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Angelic Gift"); // Copy this
+        setChoice(playerA, "Grizzly Bears"); // Attach to Grizzly Bears
+
+        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
+        setStrictChooseMode(true);
+        execute();
+
+        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
+        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 2 + 2, 2 + 2); // +2/+2 from two Angelic Gifts
+    }
+}

+import org.junit.Test;

+        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
+        // Crusade - Enchantment: White creatures get +1/+1.
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Crusade", 1);
+
+        // Cast Estrid's Invocation, copying Crusade
+        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use the copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Crusade"); // Copy Crusade

+

+        // After return, choose to copy Crusade again

+        setChoice(playerA, "Crusade"); // Copy Crusade

+    }

+package org.mage.test.cards.copy;
+
+import mage.constants.PhaseStep;
+import mage.constants.Zone;
+import org.junit.Test;
+import org.mage.test.serverside.base.CardTestPlayerBase;
+
+public class EstridTest3 extends CardTestPlayerBase {
+
+    @Test
+    public void testEstridsInvocationMultipleUses() {
+        // Estrid's Invocation
+        addCard(Zone.HAND, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation", 1);
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Island", 3);
+        // Glorious Anthem - Enchantment: Creatures you control get +1/+1.
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Glorious Anthem", 1);
+        addCard(Zone.BATTLEFIELD, playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 1);
+
+        // Turn 1: Cast Estrid's Invocation, copy Glorious Anthem
+        castSpell(1, PhaseStep.PRECOMBAT_MAIN, playerA, "Estrid's Invocation");
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this
+
+        // Turn 3 upkeep (PlayerA's next turn): Use ability
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
+        
+        // After return, choose to copy again
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this
+
+        // Turn 5 upkeep: Use ability again (second time)
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, exile and return
+        
+        // After return, choose to copy again
+        setChoice(playerA, true); // Yes, use copy effect
+        setChoice(playerA, "Glorious Anthem"); // Copy this
+
+        setStopAt(5, PhaseStep.BEGIN_COMBAT);
+        setStrictChooseMode(true);
+        execute();
+
+        // Should have 2 Glorious Anthems (the original + Estrid's Invocation as a copy)
+        assertPermanentCount(playerA, "Glorious Anthem", 2);
+        assertPowerToughness(playerA, "Grizzly Bears", 4, 4); // 2 base + 2 from two Anthems
+    }
+}
